<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>59</h3>

<p>Peering into the darkness, you notice that rough stairs have been cut into the earth and that the mouth of the cave is in fact the entrance to a tunnel.</p>
<p>Carefully descending the slippery stairway, you notice a small silver box on a shelf at the bottom of the staircase.</p>
<p class="choice">If you want to open the silver box, <a href="sect124.htm">turn to 124</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to return to the surface and press on, <a href="sect106.htm">turn to 106</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to investigate the tunnel further, <a href="sect211.htm">turn to 211</a>.</p>

</div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 60</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />

<!--

   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.
   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>60</h3>

<p>The last thing you remember before darkness engulfs you is the flash of a long curved steel knife. You have become yet another victim of the Sage and his robber son—the very one who has just slit your throat!</p>
<p class="deadend">Your quest ends here.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 61</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />
</head>

<!-- 
   Text copyright © 1984 Joe Dever.
   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.
   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>61</h3>

<p>At last you can reach the wooden fieldworks surrounding the outer city. As you race towards a sentry post, you can hear the excited shouts of the guards cheering you on. Thank the gods that they recognize you, for you must appear a ragged and suspicious figure. Your cloak is torn and hangs in tatters, your face is scratched and blood-smeared, and the dust of the Graveyard covers you from head to toe.</p>
<p>Splashing through a shallow stream, you stagger towards the gate. The full horror of the Graveyard encounter begins to catch up with you. The last thing you recall before exhaustion robs you of consciousness, is falling into the outstretched arms of two soldiers who have run from the fieldworks to help you.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect268.htm">Turn to 268</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

   Text copyright © 1984 Joe Dever.<br />
   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.<br />
  </p>

</div>

</html><!DOCTYPE html PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD XHTML 1.0 Transitional//EN" "http://www.w3.org/TR/xhtml1/DTD/xhtml1-transitional.dtd">

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 62</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />
</head>

<!-- 
   Text copyright © 1984 Joe Dever.
   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.
   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>62</h3>

<p>The ‘soldiers’ lie dead at your feet. They were bandits who were stealing from the refugees of Toran, and from the abandoned houses and farms in the area.</p>
<p>Searching their bodies you find 28 Gold Crowns and two Backpacks containing enough food for 3 Meals. They had been armed with a crossbow and three Swords. The crossbow has been damaged in the fight, but the Swords are untouched and you may keep one if you wish.</p>
<p>You adjust your equipment, give a cautious glance towards the west, and continue your run towards the outer defences of the capital.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect288.htm">Turn to 288</a>.</p>

</div>

<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>63</h3>

<p>The wild old man is screaming at you. He blames you for the war and curses the Kai Lords as agents of the Darklords. He will not listen to reason and you must fight him.</p>
<div class="illustration"><div align="center">
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0">
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpl.png" /></td>

<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="341" width="32" src="brdrl.png" /></td>
<td><a href="ill6.htm"><img alt="illustration" border="0" align="middle" height="341" width="193" src="ill6.png" /></a></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="341" width="32" src="brdrr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="193" src="brdrbt.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtr.png" /></td>
</tr>
</table>
</div></div>
<p class="combat">Madman: <span class="smallcaps">COMBAT SKILL</span> 11   <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> 10</p>
<p class="choice">If you win, <a href="sect269.htm">turn to 269</a>.</p>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>64</h3>

<p>You are awoken by the cries of a Kraan circling above the caravan. It is early morning and the sky is clear and bright. You can see a pack of Doomwolves less than a quarter of a mile away along the highway ahead. They are preparing to attack. You must act quickly.</p>
<p class="choice">If you decide to gather your equipment and run for the cover of the trees, <a href="sect188.htm">turn to 188</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you decide to cut free one of the horses and try to break through the attacking Doomwolves to the clear road beyond, then <a href="sect16.htm">turn to 16</a>.</p>

</div>

<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>65</h3>

<p>Your senses scream at you that this place is very evil. Leave as quickly as you can.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect104.htm">Turn to 104</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>66</h3>

<p>Startled, you turn around to see a burly sergeant and two soldiers running towards you, their swords drawn as if to strike.</p>
<p>You prepare to defend yourself for it looks as if they are about to attack first and ask questions later; but suddenly the sergeant calls his men to a halt. He has recognized your cloak. They put away their weapons and apologize many times for their mistake. The sergeant orders one of the men to fetch the captain of the Guard as he leads you to the doors of the Great Hall.</p>
<p>You are greeted by a tall and handsome warrior who listens intently to your story. When you have finished the account of your perilous journey to the capital, you notice a tear in the brave man’s eye as he bids you to follow him. You walk through the splendid halls and corridors of the inner Palace. The richness and grandeur are a wonder to behold. You eventually arrive at a large carved door, guarded by two soldiers wearing silver armour.</p>
<p>You are about to meet the King.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect350.htm">Turn to 350</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>67</h3>

<p>Your Kai Discipline of Tracking reveals to you fresh paw prints leading off along the south path.</p>
<p>They are the prints of a black bear, an animal renowned for its ferocity. You decide the east path would be a much safer route.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect252.htm">Turn to 252</a>.</p>

</div>

<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>68</h3>

<p>After a short walk, you reach a junction where a path crosses your present route heading from west to east.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to turn west, <a href="sect130.htm">go to 130</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to head east, <a href="sect15.htm">turn to 15</a>.</p>

<h3>69</h3>

<p>You are very near a friendly village.</p>
<p class="choice">Avoid the gallowbrush and <a href="sect272.htm">turn to 272</a>.</p>

<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>70</h3>

<p>You have reached a small bridge. A track follows the stream towards the east. A much narrower path disappears into thick forest towards the south.</p>
<div class="illustration"><div align="center">
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0">
<tr>

</tr>

</div></div>
<p class="choice">If you wish to use the Kai Discipline of Sixth Sense, <a href="sect8.htm">turn to 8</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to go east, <a href="sect28.htm">turn to 28</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to go south, <a href="sect157.htm">turn to 157</a>.</p>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>71</h3>

<p>You are winded but not hurt. You have fallen fifteen feet or so through the roof of an underground tomb. The walls are sheer and you cannot climb them. An arched tunnel leads out of the tomb towards the east, in front of which lies the sarcophagus of some ancient noble.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to use the Kai Discipline of Sixth Sense, <a href="sect65.htm">turn to 65</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to open the sarcophagus to see if it contains any treasure, <a href="sect242.htm">turn to 242</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to leave via the tunnel, <a href="sect104.htm">turn to 104</a>.</p>

</div>

<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>72</h3>

<p>You turn to face a sneering Giak and the razor-fanged jaws of its mount. You must fight them as one enemy.</p>
<p class="combat">Giak + Doomwolf: <span class="smallcaps">COMBAT SKILL</span> 15   <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> 24</p>
<p class="choice">If you win, <a href="sect265.htm">turn to 265</a>.</p>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 73</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>73</h3>

<p>Pulling your green cloak about you, you blend into the foliage and rocks. Peering carefully up at the track, you are shocked to see that they are not the King’s men at all.</p>
<p>They are Drakkarim, some of the Darklords’ cruellest troops. They must have disguised themselves as soldiers of the King in order to get this far into the forest. Thanking your Kai training for saving your life, you silently slip away from the stream and push on into the forest.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect243.htm">Turn to 243</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.<br />

</div>

<title>Flight from the Dark: 74</title>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>74</h3>

<p>The Kraan and its riders land on the track barely ten feet from where you are hidden.</p>
<p>The Giaks leap from the scaly backs of the Kraan and move towards you, their spears raised to strike. You have been seen.</p>
<p class="choice">If you decide to fight them, <a href="sect138.htm">turn to 138</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you decide to run deeper into the forest without delay, <a href="sect281.htm">turn to 281</a>.</p>

</div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 75</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />

<!--

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>75</h3>

<p>Peering out carefully, you can see three green-clad men on horses racing along the bank. You recognize them as Border Rangers, the regiment of the King’s Army that police the western borders. One of them is wounded and is slumped over the neck of his horse.</p>
<p>Close behind follow a pack of twenty Doomwolves. Their Giak riders are firing arrows at the rangers which fall all around them. One ranger drops from his horse and rolls down the river bank, a black arrow deeply embedded in his right leg.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to help the ranger, <a href="sect260.htm">turn to 260</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to stay hidden and drift downstream, <a href="sect163.htm">turn to 163</a>.</p>

</div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 76</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>76</h3>

<p>The Gem feels very hot and burns your hand. Lose 2 <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> points. You quickly grab it with the edge of your cloak and slip this Vordak Gem into your Backpack. A Gem that size must be worth hundreds of Crowns! You smile at your good fortune, mount your horse, and ride off along the south track.</p>
<div class="illustration"><div align="center">

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 77</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />

<!--

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>77</h3>

<p>The Mountain Giaks are unaccustomed to pursuing their prey through forests and you soon outdistance them, until finally the sound of their grunts and curses disappears completely.</p>
<p>When you are satisfied that they have given up the chase, you stop for a few minutes to catch your breath and check your equipment. With the memory of your ruined monastery still blazing in your mind, you gather up your meagre belongings and push on.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect19.htm">Turn to 19</a>.</p>

</div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 78</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />

<!--

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>78</h3>

<p>As the caravan careers past, you leap for the tailboard and manage to hold fast. Pulling yourself upright, you find that you are standing on the bottom rung of a ladder leading to the rear door of the wagon. Suddenly the top half of the door flies open and you are confronted by the angry face of a bodyguard.</p>
<p class="choice">If you decide to inform him that you are a Kai Lord with an urgent message for the King, <a href="sect132.htm">turn to 132</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you decide to offer him Gold Crowns for safe passage to the capital, <a href="sect12.htm">turn to 12</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you decide to attack the guard with your weapon, <a href="sect220.htm">turn to 220</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>79</h3>

<p>You come to a small footbridge across a fast-flowing stream. On the other side of the bridge the path turns south. You cross the bridge and follow the path.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect204.htm">Turn to 204</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<title>Flight from the Dark: 80</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>80</h3>

<p>You stumble backwards through the front door, clutching your burnt chest with both hands. Smoke is billowing from the shop and you must run—before the Sage or his robber son catch you.</p>
<p>You make it back to the main street and lose yourself in the rush of the crowds.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect7.htm">Turn to 7</a>.</p>

</div>

<title>Flight from the Dark: 81</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />

<!--

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>81</h3>

<p>After nearly an hour, the Kraan and their cruel riders vanish towards the west. As the shocked refugees start to emerge from the woods, you can hear the sound of horses in the distance galloping nearer. You stay hidden and wait as the riders come closer. They are the cavalry of the King’s Guard wearing the white uniforms of His Majesty’s army.</p>
<div class="illustration"><div align="center">
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0">
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="386" src="brdrtp.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="150" width="32" src="brdrl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="[illustration]" border="0" align="middle" height="150" width="386" src="small6.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="150" width="32" src="brdrr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="386" src="brdrbt.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtr.png" /></td>
</tr>
</table>
</div></div>
<p class="choice">If you wish to call to them, <a href="sect183.htm">turn to 183</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you would rather continue along the forest edge towards the south, <a href="sect200.htm">turn to 200</a>.</p>

</div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 82</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />
</head>

<!-- 
   Text copyright © 1984 Joe Dever.
   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.
   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>82</h3>

<p>The giant Gourgaz lies dead at your feet. His evil followers hiss at you and then fall back from the bridge. The Prince’s soldiers form a protective wall around you and their dying leader with their shields. Black arrows whistle past your head.</p>
<p>The dying Prince looks up into your eyes and says, ‘Kai Lord, you must take a message to my father. The enemy is too strong, we cannot hold him. The King must seek that which is in Durenor or all is lost. Take my horse and ride for the capital. May the luck of the gods ride with you.’</p>
<p>You bid a sad farewell to the Prince, mount his white steed, and head south along the forest path. The battle still rages behind you as the Prince’s men fight off another assault on the bridge.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect235.htm">Turn to 235</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 83</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />
</head>

<!-- 
   Text copyright © 1984 Joe Dever.
   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.
   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>83</h3>

<p>You have run about a mile when three soldiers appear from beneath a small footbridge. They demand that you halt and drop your weapons and equipment.</p>
<p>They are bloodstained and unshaven. Their leader is wearing the tunic of a soldier of the Toran garrison.</p>
<p class="choice">If you possess the Kai Discipline of Sixth Sense, <a href="sect45.htm">turn to 45</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to do as they say, <a href="sect205.htm">turn to 205</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to prepare to fight them, <a href="sect180.htm">turn to 180</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you demand to know what they want, <a href="sect232.htm">turn to 232</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 84</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />
</head>

<!-- 
   Text copyright © 1984 Joe Dever.

   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>84</h3>

<p>Just as you feel the air beating on your back, you slip free of your horse and roll over—landing with a splash in a muddy ditch by the side of the highway.</p>
<p>You are uninjured, and you quickly scramble to your feet and make a dash for the cover of the trees—but with thirty yards left to run, you see the Kraan circling above for another dive.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect188.htm">Turn to 188</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 85</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>85</h3>

<p>The path is wide and leads straight into thick undergrowth. The trees are tall here and unusually quiet. You walk for over a mile when suddenly you hear the beating of large wings directly above you. Looking up, you are shocked to see the sinister black outline of a Kraan diving to attack you.</p>
<p class="choice">If you draw your weapon and prepare to fight, <a href="sect229.htm">turn to 229</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you evade the attack by running south, deeper into the forest, <a href="sect99.htm">turn to 99</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 86</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>86</h3>

<p>You soon reach another crossroads.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to journey east, <a href="sect6.htm">turn to 6</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to head north, <a href="sect35.htm">turn to 35</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you prefer to go south, <a href="sect167.htm">turn to 167</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">Or if you wish to turn west, <a href="sect42.htm">turn to 42</a>.</p>

</div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 87</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />
</head>

<!-- 
   Text copyright © 1984 Joe Dever.
   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.
   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>87</h3>

<p>Focusing your powers on the lock, you try to visualize the inner mechanism. Gradually its image appears in your mind’s eye. It is old and corroded but it still functions. You are in danger of losing your concentration when a subtle <i>click</i> confirms that your effort has not been in vain.</p>
<p>The pin is an easier task. Slowly it rises out of the lock and falls to the floor. The granite door swings towards you on hidden hinges and the grey half-light of the Graveyard floods into the tomb. The exit is overgrown with graveweed and you suffer many small cuts to your face and hands as you fight your way through to the surface. You are startled by a sudden noise. You turn to see the disembodied head of a corpse laughing at you.</p>
<p>In blind panic, you race through the eerie necropolis towards the southern gate.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect61.htm">Turn to 61</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 88</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />
</head>

<!-- 
   Text copyright © 1984 Joe Dever.
   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.
   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>88</h3>

<p>You cautiously peer around the rock to see a soldier lying on his back. By his side is a Spear and shield. On the shield is the painting of a white pegasus—the Prince of Sommerlund’s emblem. He is one of the Prince’s soldiers, and he is only just conscious. His uniform is badly torn, and you can see that he has a deep wound in his left arm. As you move nearer, his eyes flicker open. ‘Heal me, my lord,’ he begs. ‘I can barely feel my arm.’</p>
<p class="choice">If you possess and wish to use the Kai Discipline of Healing on this man, <a href="sect216.htm">turn to 216</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you do not possess the skill, or if you do not want to use it, then <a href="sect31.htm">turn to 31</a>.</p>

</div>

   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.<br />
  </p>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 89</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>89</h3>

<p>In a cloud of dust and loose rocks you career down the steep hillside. The Kraan is still circling above as if waiting to direct the Giaks after you.</p>
<p>Pick a number from the <a href="random.htm">Random Number Table</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you have picked 0–1, <a href="sect53.htm">turn to 53</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If it is 2–4, <a href="sect274.htm">turn to 274</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If it is 5–9, <a href="sect316.htm">turn to 316</a>.</p>

</div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 90</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />

<!--

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>90</h3>

<p>Night falls and you are soon engulfed in total darkness. To press on would be useless, for you would be sure to lose your way. Tethering your horse to a tree, you pull your green Kai cloak about you and fall into a restless sleep.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect18.htm">Turn to 18</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 91</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />
</head>

<!-- 
   Text copyright © 1984 Joe Dever.
   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.
   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>91</h3>

<p>The small shop is dark and musty. Books and bottles of every size and colour fill the many shelves. As you close the door, a small black dog begins to yap at you. A bald man appears from behind a large screen and bids you welcome. He politely enquires as to the nature of your visit and offers you a choice of his wares from the glass counter.</p>
<div class="illustration"><div align="center">
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0">
<tr>

</div></div>
<p class="choice">If you have the Kai Discipline of Sixth Sense, <a href="sect198.htm">turn to 198</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to look at his wares, <a href="sect152.htm">turn to 152</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you would rather decline his offer and return to the street, <a href="sect7.htm">turn to 7</a>.</p>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 92</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />
</head>

<!-- 
   Text copyright © 1984 Joe Dever.
   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.
   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>92</h3>

<p>You dive for cover not a moment too soon, for a hail of black arrows scream out of the woods and bombard the area where you were standing seconds before. Pulling your cloak around you to blend into the dense bracken, you dash through the forest and away from the hidden ambushers as fast as possible. This entire area is infested by Giaks and you must escape as quickly as you can. You run without rest for over an hour until you happen to fall upon a straight forest path heading towards the east. You follow the path, taking care to keep watch for signs of the enemy.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect13.htm">Turn to 13</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 93</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />
</head>

<!-- 
   Text copyright © 1984 Joe Dever.
   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.
   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>93</h3>

<p>You turn and run for the stairs just as a large block falls with a crash behind you. The room you were in has been completely sealed off. As you escape into the daylight, you glimpse behind you the crooked figure of an old druid as he raises his staff. A second later, a bolt of lightning explodes at your feet. You do not stop but run headlong down the hill, cursing the delay but thankful for your Sixth Sense.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect106.htm">Turn to 106</a>.</p>

</div>

</head>

<!-- 
   Text copyright © 1984 Joe Dever.
   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.
   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>94</h3>

<p>The Sage, seeing that you have killed his son, turns and runs from the shop by a back door.</p>
<p>You find 12 Gold Crowns in the robber’s purse and another 4 Gold Crowns in a wooden box under the counter. Carefully examining the potions and the wand you soon realize that they are all cheap counterfeits. In fact the entire shop is full of imitations. You shake your head and return to the main street.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect7.htm">Turn to 7</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>
</div><p class="copyright">
   Text copyright © 1984 Joe Dever.<br />
   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.<br />
  </p>

<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>95</h3>

<p>You soon stumble upon a narrow forest track running from north to south.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to set off along the track towards the north, <a href="sect240.htm">turn to 240</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to go south instead, <a href="sect5.htm">turn to 5</a>.</p>

</div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 96</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>96</h3>

<p>Holding your breath, you tighten your grip on your weapon and prepare to strike. The tension is unbearable—the Giaks are so close that the foul stench of their unwashed bodies fills your nostrils. You hear them curse in their strange alien tongue and then leave the ledge and start to scramble towards the peak. When you are sure they have gone, you finally exhale and wipe the sweat from your eyes.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to explore the cave further, <a href="sect33.htm">turn to 33</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to leave the cave and descend the hill in case the Giaks return, <a href="sect248.htm">turn to 248</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.<br />

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 97</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />

<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>97</h3>

<p>Ahead of you, you can see a fierce battle raging across a stone bridge. The clash of steel and the cries of men and beasts echo through the forest. In the midst of the fighting, you see Prince Pelathar, the King’s son. He is in combat with a large grey Gourgaz who is wielding a black axe above his scaly head. Suddenly, the Prince falls wounded—a black arrow in his side.</p>
<div class="illustration"><div align="center">
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0">
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpl.png" /></td>

</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtl.png" /></td>

</tr>
</table>
</div></div>
<p class="choice">If you wish to defend the fallen Prince, <a href="sect255.htm">turn to 255</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to run into the forest, <a href="sect306.htm">turn to 306</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>98</h3>

<p>The guards seem to believe your story and bow with respect to your rank of Kai Lord. One of them pulls a concealed bell-rope and the huge doors start to swing open. They usher you inside and you hear the doors close behind you.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect139.htm">Turn to 139</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<title>Flight from the Dark: 99</title>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>99</h3>

<p>You dive into the undergrowth just as the beast screams past your head. You quickly look back to see the Kraan turning in the air in preparation for another dive. You scramble to your feet and run deeper into the safety of the forest.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect222.htm">Turn to 222</a>.</p>

</div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 100</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />

<!-- 
   Text copyright © 1984 Joe Dever.

   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>100</h3>

<p>The cold corridor suddenly makes an abrupt turning towards the east. You notice a greenish glow that lights the tunnel in the far distance. As you creep nearer you can see that the corridor opens out into a larger chamber.</p>
<p>The strange light seems to emanate from a large bowl resting upon the top of a granite throne. On a plinth in front of the throne stands a statue. It looks like a winged serpent curved in the shape of an ‘S’.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to sit on the throne, <a href="sect161.htm">turn to 161</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to examine the statue, <a href="sect133.htm">turn to 133</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to look for an exit from this chamber, <a href="sect257.htm">turn to 257</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.<br />
  </p>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 101</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />
</head>

<!-- 
   Text copyright © 1984 Joe Dever.
   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.
   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>101</h3>

<p>The noise of battle soon fades behind you but the ensuing silence is broken by a voice in your head that accuses you of being a coward, and deserting a fellow human in danger. You try to rid yourself of your nagging conscience by telling yourself that your mission is far more important, and that not only is the life of the young magician in peril but the lives of all your countrymen depend on you reaching the capital alive.</p>
<p>Suddenly, the sight of a Giak war party in the distance makes you quickly take cover and hide. But it is too late—they have spotted you and you must run as fast as you can.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect281.htm">Turn to 281</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<title>Flight from the Dark: 102</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>102</h3>

<p>As you descend the rocky slope towards the Graveyard of the Ancients, you are aware of a strange mist and cloud that swirls all around this grey and forbidding place, blocking the sun and covering the Graveyard in a perpetual gloom. A chill creeps forward to greet your approach.</p>
<p>With a feeling of deep dread, you enter the eerie necropolis.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect284.htm">Turn to 284</a>.</p>

</div>

<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>103</h3>

<p>The overgrown path leads to a junction where another track branches off towards the east.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to take this path, <a href="sect13.htm">turn to 13</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you would rather continue towards the northeast, <a href="sect287.htm">turn to 287</a>.</p>

</div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 104</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>104</h3>

<p>The walls are dank and slimy. The stale air chokes you and cobwebs brush across your face. You can feel panic grip your stomach, as the tunnel gets darker and darker.</p>
<p>You reach a junction where the tunnel meets a corridor leading from north to south.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to turn north, <a href="sect26.htm">go to 26</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to go south, <a href="sect100.htm">turn to 100</a>.</p>

</div>

   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>105</h3>

<p>In the distance, perched on the branch of an old oak tree is a jet-black raven.</p>
<div class="illustration"><div align="center">
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0">
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="386" src="brdrtp.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="150" width="32" src="brdrl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="[illustration]" border="0" align="middle" height="150" width="386" src="small8.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="150" width="32" src="brdrr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="386" src="brdrbt.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtr.png" /></td>
</tr>
</table>
</div></div>
<p class="choice">If you have the Kai Discipline of Animal Kinship, you may call to this bird by <a href="sect298.htm">turning to 298</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you do not possess this skill, or if you do not wish to use it, <a href="sect335.htm">turn to 335</a>.</p>

</div>

<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>106</h3>

<p>Eventually you come to the edge of a fast-flowing icy stream. The white water cascades over the mossy rocks and disappears towards the east.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to follow the stream to the east, <a href="sect263.htm">turn to 263</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you would rather explore upstream, <a href="sect334.htm">turn to 334</a>.</p>

</div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 107</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>107</h3>

<p>Running across the room, you lash out at the skulls, smashing them to fragments. You notice that inside each skull is a bubbling grey jelly that seems to writhe and change its shape, sprouting bat-like wings and suckers from its glistening form. In horror and loathing, you race for the exit corridor and escape just as a heavy portcullis falls with a crash, completely sealing off the chamber.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect23.htm">Turn to 23</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 108</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>108</h3>

<p>You fly in an arc through the air towards the opposite roof. Everything seems to be happening in slow motion. You see the teeming crowds below in the street, and a nest of callysparrows in the eaves of a roof to your right. You hear their startled cries as you land with a crash on the other side. But it is the last sound that you will ever hear. The tiles splinter and collapse and you fall through the four floors of the ‘Green Slipper Inn’ breaking your back in several places.</p>
<p class="deadend">Your mission and your life end here.</p>

</div>

<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>109</h3>

<p>The only thing under the carpet is dirt!</p>
<p class="choice">You may take a closer look at the bottles by <a href="sect164.htm">turning to 164</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">Or you can leave the room and investigate the stable by <a href="sect308.htm">turning to 308</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>110</h3>

<p>You quickly take aim and hurl the rock at the Giak’s head as hard as you can, but to your horror the creature ducks and the rock arcs harmlessly over its back. You must act immediately to save the wizard.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect55.htm">Turn to 55</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>111</h3>

<p>Only a few minutes after leaving the junction, you see in the distance a small log cabin and stable. On arrival you check the interior through a side window. The cabin looks deserted.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to enter the cabin, <a href="sect57.htm">turn to 57</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to search the stable, <a href="sect308.htm">turn to 308</a>.</p>

</div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 112</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>112</h3>

<p>Suddenly, the large rock you are hiding behind is rolled aside and you are faced by two snarling Giaks intent on your death. The cave mouth is a narrow entrance and you can only fight the Giaks one at a time.</p>
<div class="illustration"><div align="center">
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0">
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="386" src="brdrtp.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="150" width="32" src="brdrl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="[illustration]" border="0" align="middle" height="150" width="386" src="small9.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="150" width="32" src="brdrr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="386" src="brdrbt.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtr.png" /></td>
</tr>
</table>
</div></div>
<p class="combat">Giak 1: <span class="smallcaps">COMBAT SKILL</span> 13   <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> 10</p>
<p class="combat">Giak 2: <span class="smallcaps">COMBAT SKILL</span> 12   <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> 10</p>
<p class="choice">If you win, you may explore the cave further by <a href="sect33.htm">turning to 33</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">Or you may leave and descend the hill. <a href="sect248.htm">Turn to 248</a>.</p>

</div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 113</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />

<!--

   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.
   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>113</h3>

<p>You have been walking for over half an hour when your eye is caught by some bright red flowers growing near to a mossy bank. You recognize the plants to be Laumspur, a rare and beautiful herb much prized for its healing properties.</p>
<p>Kneeling down, you pick a handful of Laumspur and place it in your Backpack. You may eat this herb to regain lost <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> points. Each Meal of Laumspur will restore 3 <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> points, and you have gathered enough for two such Meals.<sup><a href="#sect113-1-foot" name="sect113-1">1</a></sup> Closing your pack, you continue your mission.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to head northeast, <a href="sect347.htm">turn to 347</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to head east, <a href="sect295.htm">turn to 295</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>
</div><div id="footnotes">
<p>[<a name="sect113-1-foot" href="#sect113-1">1</a>] Each Meal of Laumspur may be consumed when prompted for a Meal, in which case it fulfils the Meal requirement in addition to restoring 3 <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> points. Laumspur may also be consumed at any other time to restore <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> without having any significance as a Meal.</p></div>
<p class="copyright">
   Text copyright © 1984 Joe Dever.<br />
   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.<br />

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 114</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>114</h3>

<p>You coax the horse to lie down and begin to cover him and yourself with branches and dead leaves. You hear the wings of the Kraan as it passes over the trees. It returns and circles above you, but soon retreats back across the lake.</p>
<p>You decide to leave now, in case it returns with some of its friends.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect239.htm">Turn to 239</a>.</p>

</div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 115</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />
</head>

<!-- 
   Text copyright © 1984 Joe Dever.
   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.
   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>115</h3>

<p>You stumble into the first building and fall to the floor exhausted. You can smell cooked meat. You notice a small cauldron hanging over the embers of a dying fire, and a large oak table that has been set for a meal. Whoever lived here must have left in a great hurry this very morning. There is water in a jug and a loaf of fresh bread on the table.</p>
<div class="illustration"><div align="center">
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0">
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="386" src="brdrtp.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="150" width="32" src="brdrl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="[illustration]" border="0" align="middle" height="150" width="386" src="small10.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="150" width="32" src="brdrr.png" /></td>
</tr>

<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtl.png" /></td>

<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtr.png" /></td>
</tr>
</table>
</div></div>
<p class="choice">If you decide to take a quick Meal, <a href="sect150.htm">turn to 150</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you decide to search the building, <a href="sect177.htm">turn to 177</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you would rather leave now and continue your run, <a href="sect83.htm">turn to 83</a>.</p>

</div>

<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>116</h3>

<p>As you climb out of the muddy water, black arrows fall all around you. Quickly, you dash for the cover of the trees and wait for the Giaks to leave the opposite bank, before continuing on foot towards the capital.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect321.htm">Turn to 321</a>.</p>

</div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 117</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>117</h3>

<p>The man is badly injured and near to death. If you have the Kai Discipline of Healing, you may ease the pain of his wounds but he has been so seriously hurt he is beyond repair by your skills alone. He soon lapses into unconsciousness. You try to make him as comfortable as possible beneath a large forest oak, before leaving and pressing on through the thick woodland towards the northeast.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect330.htm">Turn to 330</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 118</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>118</h3>

<p>You spur your horse to a gallop and race down the long straight path. In the far distance you can just make out the silhouette of Holmgard on the horizon, its high walls and tall spires glinting in the morning sun. Your path joins a highway running from north to south. It is the main turnpike road between the northern port of Toran and the capital. You set off towards Holmgard, your eyes peeled for Kraan in the clear morning sky.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect224.htm">Turn to 224</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 119</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />

<!--

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>119</h3>

<p>The gallowbrush tears your cloak and scratches deep into your arms and legs as you slowly force your way through. Fifteen minutes later you emerge from the briars and stagger onwards between the trees.</p>
<p>Deduct 2 <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> points from your current score for the wounds you have sustained.</p>
<p>You feel a little dizzy as you push on, and your eyelids seem very heavy. You suddenly find yourself at the edge of a steep wooded slope.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to slide down the slope as carefully as you can, <a href="sect226.htm">turn to 226</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you do not feel that you are up to the risk of this tricky descent in your present sleepy state, walk around the edge of the ridge by <a href="sect38.htm">turning to 38</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 120</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>120</h3>

<p>Behind you can hear the blood-crazy Giaks killing the caravan horses. You risk a quick glance over your shoulder and see a Kraan start to climb high into the air. Will it attack you or is it interested in something else? The dark shadow that is gradually getting larger all around you tells you that you are its intended victim. The Kraan is diving full speed at you!</p>
<p class="choice">If you wait until it is about to strike and then jump from the saddle, <a href="sect84.htm">turn to 84</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you head as fast as you can for the trees, <a href="sect171.htm">turn to 171</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you put your head down, pray to the heavens for good luck and gallop on regardless, <a href="sect54.htm">turn to 54</a>.</p>

</div>

<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>121</h3>

<p>After a few minutes walking you see a stranger, clad in red, standing in the centre of the track ahead. He has his back towards you, and his head is covered by the hood of his robes. Perched on his outstretched arm is the black raven that you saw earlier.</p>
<div class="illustration"><div align="center">
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0">
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpl.png" /></td>

<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="339" width="32" src="brdrl.png" /></td>
<td><a href="ill8.htm"><img alt="illustration" border="0" align="middle" height="339" width="193" src="ill8.png" /></a></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="339" width="32" src="brdrr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="193" src="brdrbt.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtr.png" /></td>
</tr>
</table>
</div></div>
<p class="choice">If you wish to call the stranger, <a href="sect342.htm">turn to 342</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to approach the stranger cautiously, <a href="sect309.htm">turn to 309</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you would rather draw your weapon and attack, <a href="sect283.htm">turn to 283</a>.</p>

</div>

<title>Flight from the Dark: 122</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>122</h3>

<p>Immediately the horse senses your communication. He calms down. You walk towards the beautiful animal and stroke his head reassuringly. You sense that he is frightened and confused. Mounting him, you lead him off to the path and head south once again.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect206.htm">Turn to 206</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>123</h3>

<p>As the creature dies, its body slowly dissolves into a vile green liquid. You notice that all of the grass and the plants beneath the smoking fluid are beginning to shrivel and die. A large valuable looking Gem lies on the ground near to the decaying body.</p>
<p>Further along the track you can see a large war party of Giaks running towards you.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to take the Gem, <a href="sect304.htm">turn to 304</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you would rather leave it and run, <a href="sect2.htm">turn to 2</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>124</h3>

<p>Inside the box you find 15 Gold Crowns and a Silver Key. If you wish to keep the key, remember to mark it on your <a href="action.htm">Action Chart</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">You can continue to investigate the tunnel by <a href="sect211.htm">turning to 211</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">Or you may leave and descend the hill by <a href="sect106.htm">turning to 106</a>.</p>

</div>

<title>Flight from the Dark: 125</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>125</h3>

<p>The path opens out into a large clearing. You notice strange claw prints in the earth. Kraan have landed here. By the number of prints and by the size of the area disturbed, you judge that at least five of the foul creatures landed here in the last twelve hours.</p>
<p>You see two exits on the far side of the clearing. One leads west, the other south.</p>
<p class="choice">If you have the Kai Discipline of Tracking, <a href="sect301.htm">turn to 301</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to take the south path, <a href="sect27.htm">turn to 27</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to take the west path, <a href="sect214.htm">turn to 214</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>126</h3>

<p>You ride deeper and deeper into the forest. Silently you thank the Prince for such a fine horse, for although the ground is a tangle of briars and roots, he never once falters. The Doomwolves are soon left far behind and you bring your horse to a halt. The light has faded fast and it is almost night.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to press on ahead, <a href="sect46.htm">turn to 46</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to bear left (the same direction as the path you left far behind) then <a href="sect143.htm">turn to 143</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>127</h3>

<p>After an hour of marching, the Drakkarim suddenly halt as a large, grey scaly creature approaches along the track. As the beast draws closer, you can smell its fetid breath on your face. It lets out a roar and grabs your head in its powerful webbed hands. The last thing you hear is the sharp crack of your spine snapping.</p>
<p class="deadend">Your quest ends here.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>128</h3>

<p>Carefully parting the dense foliage, you are horrified by the sight that meets you. In a small clearing ahead, three Giaks have tied a man to a wooden stake and are setting fire to a mass of brushwood bundled at his feet. You recognize his tunic as that of a Border Ranger, one of the King’s men who police the kingdom near the Durncrag Mountains of the west. He has been badly beaten and is nearly unconscious.</p>
<p class="choice">If you have the Kai Discipline of Hunting, <a href="sect297.htm">turn to 297</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you do not, you must attack the Giaks now in order to save the ranger’s life. <a href="sect336.htm">Turn to 336</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>129</h3>

<p>You reach the main gates of the capital, and stare in awe at the height of the city’s walls. Two hundred feet high, the walls of Holmgard have withstood the ravages of both time and the Darklords. You and the officer race through the tunnel of the inner gatehouse, one hundred yards in length, and finally halt outside the doorway of the main watchtower. Great crowds of soldiers and civilians are running to and fro.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to continue following the officer, <a href="sect3.htm">turn to 3</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you feel that you stand a better chance of making your way to the King’s citadel on your own, <a href="sect144.htm">turn to 144</a>.</p>

</div>

<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>130</h3>

<p>You soon reach a small clearing in the woods. A bench, carved from a fallen tree is set in the centre of the clearing. You are hungry and must now eat a Meal here.</p>
<div class="illustration"><div align="center">
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0">

</table>
</div></div>
<p class="choice">When you have finished, if you decide to leave the clearing by the south way, <a href="sect28.htm">turn to 28</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">Or if you prefer the smaller track that leads eastwards into the forest, <a href="sect201.htm">turn to 201</a>.</p>

</div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 131</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />

<!--
