<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>131</h3>

<p>You have covered about a quarter of a mile when you hear shouting and a noise like thunderclaps ahead. Edging nearer, you soon make out a clearing that you recognize to be the site of the ruins of Raumas, an ancient forest temple.</p>
<p>A war party of Giaks, some twenty-five to thirty strong, are attacking the ruins from all sides. Many more of the Giaks are dead or dying among the broken pillars of marble, but still they assault whatever is hidden inside. Suddenly, a bolt of blue lightning rips through the front rank of Giaks sending the armour-clad creatures tumbling in all directions. A Giak, taller than the others and dressed from head to foot in black chainmail, curses at his troops as he whips them forward with a barbed flail.</p>
<p>With weapon ready, you move to the edge of the clearing, under cover of the thick foliage, and try to catch a glimpse of the defenders. To your amazement, the ruins are being defended by a young man no older than yourself. You recognize his sky-blue robes, embroidered with stars. He is a young theurgist of the Magicians’ Guild of Toran: an apprentice in magic.</p>
<div class="illustration"><div align="center">
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0">
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="193" src="brdrtp.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="338" width="32" src="brdrl.png" /></td>
<td><a href="ill9.htm"><img alt="illustration" border="0" align="middle" height="338" width="193" src="ill9.png" /></a></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="338" width="32" src="brdrr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="193" src="brdrbt.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtr.png" /></td>
</tr>
</table>
</div></div>
<p>Five Giaks charge forward, their spears raised to stab the apprentice as he hurriedly retreats deeper into the ruins. You see him turn and raise his left hand just before a bolt of blue flame shoots from his fingertips into the snarling Giak soldiers. Close to where you are hidden, you see a Giak scuttle past and climb one of the pillars of the temple. He has a long curved dagger in his mouth and he is about to jump on the young wizard standing below.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to shout a warning to the wizard, <a href="sect241.htm">turn to 241</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to run forward and attack the Giak when he jumps, <a href="sect55.htm">turn to 55</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to pick up a chunk of temple marble and throw it at the Giak’s head, <a href="sect302.htm">turn to 302</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">Or if you would rather turn and leave the battle area and run back into the woods, <a href="sect101.htm">turn to 101</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>132</h3>

<p>The bodyguard looks at you with great suspicion and slams the door. You can hear voices chattering inside the caravan. Suddenly the door swings open and the face of a wealthy merchant appears. He recognizes your Kai cloak and apologizes for his servant’s behaviour.</p>
<p>He says that they have been attacked several times since they left Toran: by Kraan, by bandits, and by robbers. They thought you may have been a bandit. Inside, the caravan is full of silks and spices. The merchant offers you food which you gratefully accept. After your sumptuous meal, the fatigue of your ordeal finally overcomes you and you slip into a deep sleep.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect64.htm">Turn to 64</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>133</h3>

<p>As you approach the statue, several cracks appear in its stone surface. It suddenly explodes before you as a real Winged Serpent breaks free of its stone mantle and attacks you.</p>
<p>You must fight the creature.</p>
<p class="combat">Winged Serpent: <span class="smallcaps">COMBAT SKILL</span> 16   <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> 18</p>
<p>(This creature is immune to Mindblast.)</p>
<p class="choice">If you win the fight, <a href="sect266.htm">turn to 266</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>134</h3>

<p>Using your skills, you detect Giak tracks around the perimeter of the clearing. The prints are fresh and you can tell that these cruel minions of the Darklords were in this area less than two hours ago.</p>
<p class="choice">Forewarned by this knowledge, if you decide to investigate the huts, <a href="sect305.htm">turn to 305</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you would rather avoid the clearing, <a href="sect40.htm">turn to 40</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>135</h3>

<p>Peering over the steep undercut of the river bank, you can see a tangle of driftwood along the water’s edge. A large tree trunk has grounded on the clay bank next to a small canoe.</p>
<div class="illustration"><div align="center">
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0">
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="386" src="brdrtp.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="150" width="32" src="brdrl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="[illustration]" border="0" align="middle" height="150" width="386" src="small12.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="150" width="32" src="brdrr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="386" src="brdrbt.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtr.png" /></td>
</tr>
</table>
</div></div>
<p class="choice">If you wish to use the log to float down the river, <a href="sect223.htm">turn to 223</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to use the canoe, <a href="sect4.htm">turn to 4</a>.</p>

</div>

<title>Flight from the Dark: 136</title>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>136</h3>

<p>The Giaks get nearer and then crouch down as if preparing themselves to pounce. You can see the sharp serrated points of their spears and hear their low guttural speech. The larger of the two creatures screams, <i xml:lang="x-giak">‘Orgadak taag! Nogjat aga ok!’</i> and attacks you.</p>
<p>You must fight each of the Giaks in turn. Add 1 point to your <span class="smallcaps">COMBAT SKILL</span> during this fight, as you have the advantage of the higher ground in your favour.</p>
<p class="combat">Giak 1: <span class="smallcaps">COMBAT SKILL</span> 13   <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> 10</p>
<p class="combat">Giak 2: <span class="smallcaps">COMBAT SKILL</span> 12   <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> 10</p>
<p class="choice">If you win, <a href="sect313.htm">turn to 313</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>137</h3>

<p>As the last of the foul creatures die, so the greenish light starts to fade. You notice that in each of the broken skulls lies a Gem. You take these 20 Tomb Guardian Gems before darkness engulfs the chamber. Remember to mark these on your <a href="action.htm">Action Chart</a> as a single Backpack Item.</p>
<p>You quickly leave the dead Crypt spawn and press on.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect23.htm">Turn to 23</a>.</p>

</div>

<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>138</h3>

<p>You prepare your weapon and advance to meet the enemy. There are two Mountain Giaks and you must fight them one at a time.</p>
<p class="combat">Giak 1: <span class="smallcaps">COMBAT SKILL</span> 13   <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> 10</p>
<p class="combat">Giak 2: <span class="smallcaps">COMBAT SKILL</span> 12   <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> 10</p>
<p class="choice">If you win, <a href="sect291.htm">turn to 291</a>.</p>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>139</h3>

<p>The inner courtyard is a bustle of activity. Cavalry scouts are waiting beside their nervous horses for messages from their unit commanders inside the Great Hall. They take orders with great speed to the defenders of the outer fieldworks. No sooner do they gallop off, than other scouts return, many of them breathless and wounded.</p>
<p>You have taken less than a dozen steps across the courtyard when you hear a deep voice boom out. ‘Stop that man!’</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect66.htm">Turn to 66</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>140</h3>

<p>You are in a clearing where several trees have been cut down to make a rickety watchtower. Below the tower are three paths leading off in different directions.</p>
<p class="choice">If you take the south path, <a href="sect14.htm">turn to 14</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you take the east path, <a href="sect252.htm">turn to 252</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you take the southwest path, <a href="sect215.htm">turn to 215</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you decide to climb the watchtower, <a href="sect36.htm">turn to 36</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>141</h3>

<p>Your Sixth Sense has warned you that some of the creatures that attacked the monastery are searching the two paths for any survivors of their raid, but you can avoid both tracks by making your way through the undergrowth of the woods.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to head south, <a href="sect56.htm">turn to 56</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">Or if you wish to cut through the heavier foliage towards the northeast, <a href="sect333.htm">turn to 333</a>.</p>

</div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 142</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />
</head>

<!-- 
   Text copyright © 1984 Joe Dever.
   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.
   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>142</h3>

<p>You can see the tall grey-white walls and glimmering spires of Holmgard, its banners fluttering from the battlements in the fresh morning breeze. Stretching out towards the west, the River Eledil traces its course from the mountains of the Durncrag Range to the Holmgulf. But from below the mountain peaks you can see a vast black army marching relentlessly on towards the city.</p>
<p>To your right you can see the highway heading off over the rolling plain towards Holmgard. At a run you could reach the outer fieldworks of the city defences in an hour, but you would be in the open for most of the time and vulnerable to attack by Kraan. However, ahead of you, a wide and muddy river drifts sluggishly towards the Eledil. You could use the cover of the river banks and swim towards the capital. Or towards your left lies the Graveyard of the Ancients. These tombs and crumbling monuments to a forgotten age would conceal your approach, but it is a forbidden area. Many are the unnamed horrors that lie there in restless sleep, waiting to consume the unwary trespasser.</p>
<div class="illustration"><div align="center">
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0">
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="386" src="brdrtp.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="150" width="32" src="brdrl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="[illustration]" border="0" align="middle" height="150" width="386" src="small13.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="150" width="32" src="brdrr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="386" src="brdrbt.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtr.png" /></td>
</tr>
</table>
</div></div>
<p class="choice">If you will try your luck by the highway, <a href="sect58.htm">turn to 58</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you feel that you stand a better chance of reaching the capital via the river, then <a href="sect135.htm">turn to 135</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">Or if you are brave enough to risk the unknown perils of the Graveyard of the Ancients, <a href="sect102.htm">turn to 102</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>143</h3>

<p>You soon emerge from the woods onto a main highway. You recognize it as being the main road between the port of Toran in the north and the capital in the south. Spurring your horse on, you estimate you will reach the capital by morning.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect149.htm">Turn to 149</a>.</p>

</div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 144</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>144</h3>

<p>You fight your way through the press of bodies along the main street towards the citadel in the distance. City folk are rushing to and fro in the grip of panic, as the cries of Kraan are heard circling high above.</p>
<p>In the crush, one item is stolen from your Backpack. If you no longer have a Backpack or if you have no Backpack Items, you lose a Weapon. Remember to take this off your <a href="action.htm">Action Chart</a>.</p>
<p>A runaway horse and cart career past and knock you into a doorway. You are stunned and you lose 2 <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> points. As you stagger to your feet, the door bursts open and a decrepit old man attacks you with a meat cleaver. He is quite insane and you must fight him or take evasive action.</p>
<p class="choice">If you choose to fight, <a href="sect63.htm">turn to 63</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to evade a fight, <a href="sect217.htm">turn to 217</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>145</h3>

<p>You feel as if you have been run down by a cart or wagon. As you fall forward the last thing that you remember before the darkness overcomes you, is the taste of the sandy road and the terrible pain in your back.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect165.htm">Turn to 165</a>.</p>

  </p>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 146</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>146</h3>

<p>You have ridden about a mile when you are knocked from your horse by an arrow grazing your forehead. You lose 3 <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> points.</p>
<p>As you pull yourself to your feet, you see a patrol of Drakkarim emerge from the woods on either side of the road. You have been ambushed and must evade them as quickly as possible by going into the forest.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect154.htm">Turn to 154</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>147</h3>

<p>After a few minutes walking, you find a mossy hut set back from the path. You are hungry and must eat a Meal here or lose 3 <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> points. As you eat you notice that the path starts to curve towards the east. <sup><a href="#sect147-1-foot" name="sect147-1">2</a></sup></p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to follow it, <a href="sect42.htm">turn to 42</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to return the way you have come, <a href="sect28.htm">turn to 28</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>
</div><div id="footnotes">
<p>[<a name="sect147-1-foot" href="#sect147-1">2</a>] The wording of this section assumes that you have come from <a href="sect28.htm">Section 28</a>. If you have just reached this section for the first time from <a href="sect42.htm">Section 42</a>, read the last sentence and two choices as follows: ‘… As you eat you notice that the path starts to curve towards the north. If you wish to follow it, <a href="sect28.htm">turn to 28</a>. If you wish to return the way you have come, <a href="sect42.htm">turn to 42</a>.’</p></div>

<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>148</h3>

<p>Kicking open the door, you dive into the farmhouse. A Kraan soars overhead, letting out a shriek of victory, a victim hanging in its claws. Getting to your feet, you find yourself alone. But propped against the fireplace is a Warhammer. You may take this Weapon if you wish.</p>
<p class="choice">If you want to stay in the farmhouse, <a href="sect81.htm">turn to 81</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you would feel safer in the forest, you can make a dash by <a href="sect320.htm">turning to 320</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to search the room further, <a href="sect199.htm">turn to 199</a>.</p>

</div>

<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>149</h3>

<p>As you ride along the highway, you notice that light is getting worse. It will soon be completely dark—and impossible to see any dangers that may lurk ahead. You decide to hide and rest at the wood’s edge until morning.</p>
<p>When you are satisfied that no one can see you, you pull your warm green cloak about you and drift off into an uneasy sleep.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect256.htm">Turn to 256</a>.</p>

</div>

<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>150</h3>

<p>Although a little overcooked, the food tastes fine (although it is not enough for a whole Meal) and the clear water slakes your thirst. You have spent nearly half an hour resting in this house when you suddenly realize the delay.</p>
<p class="choice">Prepare your equipment and leave. <a href="sect83.htm">Turn to 83</a>.</p>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>151</h3>

<p>If you concentrate on the keyhole, you could move the mechanism of the lock and open it. You can then make the pin levitate and free it from the lockplate, avoiding falling prey to any traps that may be set off as the door unlocks.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to use your Kai Discipline of Mind Over Matter to open this lock and levitate the pin, <a href="sect87.htm">turn to 87</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to remove the pin, <a href="sect337.htm">turn to 337</a>.</p>

</div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 152</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>152</h3>

<p>The herbalist offers you a selection of special potions. Some increase your strength; some induce invisibility; some give you great powers of stealth; and others give you the power of turning yourself into a gaseous form. The man pulls open the bottom drawer of the counter to reveal a magnificent wand. He says that it is a powerful weapon against all evil creatures, and that it will make you invulnerable in battle. He points to the mystical inscriptions which cover the black staff.</p>
<div class="illustration"><div align="center">
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0">
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpl.png" /></td>

<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="324" width="32" src="brdrl.png" /></td>
<td><a href="ill10.htm"><img alt="illustration" border="0" align="middle" height="324" width="193" src="ill10.png" /></a></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="324" width="32" src="brdrr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="193" src="brdrbt.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtr.png" /></td>
</tr>
</table>
</div></div>
<p class="choice">If you wish to lean over the counter and read the strange inscriptions, <a href="sect49.htm">turn to 49</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you are more interested in the potions, <a href="sect231.htm">turn to 231</a>.</p>

</div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 153</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />
</head>

<!-- 
   Text copyright © 1984 Joe Dever.
   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.
   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>153</h3>

<p>Before you are the tall grey-white walls and glimmering spires of Holmgard, the city’s banners fluttering from the battlements in the fresh morning breeze. Stretching out towards the west, the River Eledil traces its course from the mountains of the Durncrag Range to the Holmgulf. But below the mountain peaks you can see a vast black army marching relentlessly on towards the capital.</p>
<div class="illustration"><div align="center">
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0">
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="386" src="brdrtp.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="150" width="32" src="brdrl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="[illustration]" border="0" align="middle" height="150" width="386" src="small13.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="150" width="32" src="brdrr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="386" src="brdrbt.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtr.png" /></td>
</tr>
</table>
</div></div>
<p>To your right you can see the highway heading off over the rolling plain towards Holmgard. At a gallop you could make the outer fieldworks of the city’s defences in less than an hour, but you would be in the open for most of the time and vulnerable to attack by Kraan. Directly ahead of you, a wide river drifts sluggishly towards the Eledil. If you abandoned your horse, you could swim towards the outer defences under cover of the river banks. Or there is a final alternative. To your left lies the Graveyard of the Ancients. These tombs and crumbling monuments to a forgotten age would conceal your approach but it is a forbidden area. Many are the unnamed horrors that lie there in restless sleep, waiting to consume the unwary trespasser.</p>
<p class="choice">If you will try your luck by the highway, <a href="sect202.htm">turn to 202</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you feel that you stand a better chance of reaching the capital via the river then <a href="sect135.htm">turn to 135</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">Or if you are brave enough to risk the unknown perils of the Graveyard of the Ancients, <a href="sect329.htm">turn to 329</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

  </p>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 154</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />
</head>

<!-- 
   Text copyright © 1984 Joe Dever.
   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.
   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>154</h3>

<p>You are dizzy from your wound and you stumble through the trees like a blind man.</p>
<p>Suddenly you fall forward as if the ground has been snatched from beneath your feet. You have fallen head-first into a hunting pit. As you look up, you can see four Drakkarim levelling their bows at you, evil sneers spreading simultaneously across their ugly faces.</p>
<p class="deadend">As the world darkens, the last thing you feel is the black shafts of their arrows deep in your chest. You have failed in your mission.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.<br />
  </p>

</html><!DOCTYPE html PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD XHTML 1.0 Transitional//EN" "http://www.w3.org/TR/xhtml1/DTD/xhtml1-transitional.dtd">
<html xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml" lang="en-UK" xml:lang="en-UK">

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 155</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />
</head>

<!-- 
   Text copyright © 1984 Joe Dever.
   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.
   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>155</h3>

<p>As you approach, the group of people stop talking. You can see by their expressions that they recognize your green Kai cloak. Slowly, one of the men extends his hand in friendship and says, ‘My Lord, we had heard a rumour that the Kai were destroyed. Heaven be praised that it is not so. We feared all was lost.’</p>
<p>You do not tell them of the destruction of the monastery, for they are refugees from Toran and have lost everything they owned. Their only hope now is that the Kai Lords will lead an army to victory. You learn that the northern port was attacked from both air and sea, and that the forces of the Darklords far outnumbered the King’s brave garrison. You reassure them that Sommerlund will not fall and wish them luck on their journey ahead.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect70.htm">Turn to 70</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>156</h3>

<p>Black arrows embed themselves in the mud all around you. More Giaks have appeared on the steep slope of the river bank and are firing at you. There is no cover on this side of the river.</p>
<div class="illustration"><div align="center">
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0">
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpl.png" /></td>

<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="150" width="32" src="brdrl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="[illustration]" border="0" align="middle" height="150" width="386" src="small14.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="150" width="32" src="brdrr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="386" src="brdrbt.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtr.png" /></td>
</tr>
</table>
</div></div>
<p class="choice">If you wish to dive into the water and swim with the current, <a href="sect294.htm">turn to 294</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to swim across to the cover of the trees on the other bank, <a href="sect245.htm">turn to 245</a>.</p>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>157</h3>

<p>The forest begins to thin out until finally you can make out a road through the trees ahead. The highway is full of people heading south. Many are wheeling their possessions along on handcarts.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to join the refugees and perhaps learn more of what has happened in the north, <a href="sect30.htm">turn to 30</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you would prefer to continue to move south but under cover of the trees, <a href="sect167.htm">turn to 167</a>.</p>

</div>

<title>Flight from the Dark: 158</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>158</h3>

<p>The Key fits and the lock opens. You pull back the door to find yourself face to face with a strange old man. In his right hand is a staff. Suddenly a bolt of lightning shoots from the staff and hits you square in the chest. You lose 6 <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> points. Gasping with pain, you knock the old man aside and run up the steep staircase towards daylight. You are halfway up the stairs when he fires another bolt at you.</p>
<p>Pick a number from the <a href="random.htm">Random Number Table</a>.</p>
<p>If the number is 0–5, the bolt misses you and shatters part of the wall.</p>
<p>If the number is 6–9, then you have been hit in the back and lose a further 4 <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> points.</p>
<p>If you survive, you stagger out into the daylight and curse your bad luck. It was only by an unlucky chance you discovered the secret temple of a sect of evil druids. You are very lucky to have escaped with your life. You quickly rejoin the path which now disappears over the hill.</p>

<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="150" width="32" src="brdrl.png" /></td>

</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="386" src="brdrbt.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtr.png" /></td>
</tr>
</table>
</div></div>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect106.htm">Turn to 106</a>.</p>

<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>159</h3>

<p>Your ploy does not work, for the merchant will not allow you to enter his caravan. Suddenly he clicks his fingers and the bodyguard grasps the hilt of his scimitar.</p>
<p class="choice">You must fight him by <a href="sect191.htm">turning to 191</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">Or you must jump clear of the speeding caravan. <a href="sect234.htm">Turn to 234</a>.</p>

<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>160</h3>

<p>Pick a number from the <a href="random.htm">Random Number Table</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If it is 0–4, you have been seen. <a href="sect286.htm">Turn to 286</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If it is 5–9, they do not spot you and they slowly file away along the far side of the ridge. <a href="sect10.htm">Turn to 10</a>.</p>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>161</h3>

<p>As you sit down, the stone serpent slowly moves forward on its plinth. You suddenly break out in a cold sweat and grasp your weapon with trembling fingers in case it should attack. A red forked tongue appears from the head of this strange statue and dips into the bowl of green light above your head. Slowly the tongue re-emerges holding a Golden Key which, to your surprise, it drops into your lap. A panel in the east wall clicks open to reveal an exit.</p>
<p>You take the Key and leave as quickly as possible.</p>
<div class="illustration"><div align="center">
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0">
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="386" src="brdrtp.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="150" width="32" src="brdrl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="[illustration]" border="0" align="middle" height="150" width="386" src="small16.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="150" width="32" src="brdrr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="386" src="brdrbt.png" /></td>

</div></div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 162</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>162</h3>

<p>As you get nearer to the men, you call to them. As they turn to face you, your skin turns cold and your heart pounds, for they are Drakkarim in disguise. Suddenly they charge at you. Forced to the ground, you are tied up with ropes and dragged behind them along a track. They take your Backpack and Weapons, but do not search your cloak or find your Gold Crowns. They cackle menacingly to themselves, and talk at great length of the tortures that await you at their camp.</p>
<p class="choice">If you have the Kai Discipline of Mind Over Matter, <a href="sect258.htm">turn to 258</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you do not have this skill, <a href="sect127.htm">turn to 127</a>.</p>

</div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 163</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>163</h3>

<p>After nearly half an hour you feel the current getting stronger. Looking out across the surface you can see that you are approaching a whirlpool in the middle of a large river bend. You will surely drown if caught in its current, so you quickly swim towards the right hand river bank and continue your mission on foot, carrying all your equipment.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect321.htm">Turn to 321</a>.</p>

</div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 164</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />

<!--

   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.
   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>164</h3>

<p>Carefully opening the seals on each of the bottles, you sniff at the contents. They all seem to be different types of wine. Suddenly a smaller bottle tucked behind the others catches your eye. Pulling out the glass stopper, you recognize the smell to be that of Alether, a Potion of Strength, which is orange in colour.</p>
<p>You may keep this Potion and swallow it before you fight. It will increase your <span class="smallcaps">COMBAT SKILL</span> by 2 points for the duration of your fight. Be sure to mark it down on your <a href="action.htm">Action Chart</a> and to strike it off once you have used it.</p>
<p class="choice">You now decide to investigate the stable by <a href="sect308.htm">turning to 308</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>165</h3>

<p>You awake in a fever. Images swim before your eyes and then fade completely. The pain in your back is intense and you cry out for relief. You feel a cool, damp cloth placed on your forehead and glimpse the worried face of a young woman. An old man whispers in her ear and then he disappears from view. The girl kneels at your side and comforts you with words of kindness and reassurance, but the light quickly fades and darkness engulfs you once more.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect212.htm">Turn to 212</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<title>Flight from the Dark: 166</title>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>166</h3>

<p>You are in the presence of a great evil. Your mind is being probed by a powerful and timeless being and you must shield yourself. The struggle has begun and your sanity is at stake. It is a long and torturous ordeal, during which you experience many fantastic and terrible apparitions that tempt and appal you. After this you must lose 4 <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> points and stagger towards the tunnel.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect104.htm">Turn to 104</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>167</h3>

<p>You have been travelling for about a mile when you notice two legs sticking out from behind a large boulder.</p>
<p class="choice">If you possess and wish to use the Kai Discipline of Sixth Sense, <a href="sect178.htm">turn to 178</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to take a closer look, <a href="sect88.htm">turn to 88</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you would rather avoid meeting their owner and press on into the forest, <a href="sect264.htm">turn to 264</a>.</p>

</div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 168</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>168</h3>

<p>You pull yourself to the top of the opulent caravan and nestle among the travelling cases and bags. Night will soon engulf the highway. A chill wind blows from the west and you pull your cloak around yourself to keep warm. You listen to the voices below and you can smell the mouthwatering aroma of spiced meat. It reminds you that you are very hungry and must now take a Meal.</p>
<p>The fatigue of your ordeal finally catches up with you and you drift off into a restless sleep.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect64.htm">Turn to 64</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>169</h3>

<p>As you pass each skull, it slowly turns, as if watching your every move. You are halfway across the room when you hear the sharp crack of bone splitting. Suddenly you see hideous shapes hatching inside the skulls, and stretching their wings.</p>
<p>Ten slimy winged creatures attack you, and you must fight them as one enemy.</p>
<p class="combat">Crypt Spawn: <span class="smallcaps">COMBAT SKILL</span> 16   <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> 16</p>
<p class="choice">You may evade more fighting after the first round of combat and run for the archway by <a href="sect23.htm">turning to 23</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you win the combat, <a href="sect137.htm">turn to 137</a>.</p>

</div>

<title>Flight from the Dark: 170</title>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>170</h3>

<p>The tunnel is dark and the air is much cooler than outside. You carefully advance with one hand on the tunnel wall to aid your sense of direction. You have been in total darkness for three minutes when you detect the foul smell of decay ahead, similar to rotting meat. If you have a Torch and Tinderbox in your Pack, you may light the Torch to see your way ahead.</p>
<p>Suddenly, something heavy drops from the tunnel ceiling onto your back and you fall to your knees. It is a Burrowcrawler and you must fight it, for it is trying to strangle you with its long slimy tentacles.</p>
<div class="illustration"><div align="center">
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0">
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpl.png" /></td>

<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="333" width="32" src="brdrl.png" /></td>
<td><a href="ill11.htm"><img alt="illustration" border="0" align="middle" height="333" width="193" src="ill11.png" /></a></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="333" width="32" src="brdrr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="193" src="brdrbt.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtr.png" /></td>
</tr>
</table>
</div></div>
<p class="combat">Burrowcrawler: <span class="smallcaps">COMBAT SKILL</span> 17   <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> 7</p>
<p>If you do not have a torch, deduct 3 points from your <span class="smallcaps">COMBAT SKILL</span> during this fight. The Burrowcrawler is immune to Mindblast and Animal Kinship.</p>
<p class="choice">If you win, <a href="sect319.htm">turn to 319</a>.</p>

</div>

<title>Flight from the Dark: 171</title>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>171</h3>

<p>You are at the very edge of the wood when your horse rears up in agony. The Kraan has sunk its claws deep into the horse’s hind legs and is trying to knock you to the ground with its wings. The ghoulish Giak rider squeals with delight as he stabs at you with his spear. You jump to the ground and dash for the trees, leaving the poor dying horse in the clutches of the Kraan.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect303.htm">Turn to 303</a>.</p>

</div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 172</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>172</h3>

<p>Night falls and you are soon engulfed in darkness. To press on any further would be futile, for you would be sure to lose your way. Tethering your horse to a tree, you pull your green Kai cloak about you and fall into a restless sleep.</p>
<p>You are awoken by the sound of troops in the distance. Across the lake you see the black shapes of Drakkarim and a pack of Doomwolves. A Kraan appears from above the trees and lands on the roof of the small wooden shack. It is being ridden by a creature dressed in red robes. The Kraan takes off and begins to fly across the lake to where you are hidden.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to use the Kai Discipline of Camouflage to hide yourself and your horse, <a href="sect114.htm">turn to 114</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to ride deeper into the forest to escape the Kraan, <a href="sect239.htm">turn to 239</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to prepare to fight the creature, <a href="sect29.htm">turn to 29</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>173</h3>

<p>As you reach the door you hear the crash of a giant stone slab as it falls from the ceiling. Turning around, you see that your exit is now blocked.</p>
<p class="choice">If you have a Silver Key, you may try to open the door by <a href="sect158.htm">turning to 158</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you do not possess a Silver Key, <a href="sect259.htm">turn to 259</a>.</p>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 174</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />

<!--

   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.
   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>174</h3>

<p>After nearly an hour of drifting downstream, the water current becomes quite strong and you can see that you are being drawn towards a whirlpool near the centre as the river curves round. You know that if you are caught in the swirling water, you stand very little chance of escaping a watery death. You dive into the muddy river and as you begin to swim towards the shore you unfortunately lose your Backpack and Weapons. Without your equipment, you reach the wooded bank.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect190.htm">Turn to 190</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 175</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />

<!-- 
   Text copyright © 1984 Joe Dever.
   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.
   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>175</h3>

<p>Waving your arms at the approaching cavalry, you recognize them to be Border Rangers of the King’s army, tough woodsmen who police the troubled western frontier of the kingdom. Your relief at seeing them soon fades when you realize that they are fleeing from a pack of Doomwolves with snarling Giak riders. Black arrows are dropping all around the rangers, as the vicious Doomwolves get nearer and nearer.</p>
<p class="choice">If you possess the Kai Discipline of Camouflage, <a href="sect182.htm">turn to 182</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to take cover and hide, <a href="sect41.htm">turn to 41</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to make for the other bank, <a href="sect116.htm">turn to 116</a>.</p>

</div>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>176</h3>

<p>You hide behind some thick bushes so that the Doomwolf and its rider will not see your white horse. Luckily it works—the beast lopes past and vanishes down the track that you have just come along.</p>
<div class="illustration"><div align="center">
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0">
<tr>

<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="150" width="32" src="brdrl.png" /></td>

</tr>

<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="386" src="brdrbt.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtr.png" /></td>
</tr>
</table>
</div></div>
<p class="choice">If you wish to attack the remaining Doomwolves and their riders, <a href="sect253.htm">turn to 253</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to press on deeper into the forest, <a href="sect126.htm">turn to 126</a>.</p>

</div>

<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>177</h3>

<p>You search all of the cupboards in the small cottage but do not find anything of use or value. You decide that you have wasted enough time here and must press on without further delay.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect83.htm">Turn to 83</a>.</p>

<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>178</h3>

<p>Your skill enables you to recognize the boots and leggings of a King’s soldier. You can sense that the man is wounded and in need of help.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to aid him, <a href="sect88.htm">turn to 88</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you would rather leave him here, <a href="sect264.htm">turn to 264</a>.</p>

</div>

<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>179</h3>

<p>You have been spotted by the guards who level their crossbows at you.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to raise your hands above your head and walk slowly towards them, <a href="sect318.htm">turn to 318</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to run for cover in the trees, <a href="sect51.htm">turn to 51</a>.</p>

</div>

<title>Flight from the Dark: 180</title>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>180</h3>

<p>They see you raise your weapon, and they instantly attack you.</p>
<p>If you decide to fight them, you must fight them one at a time.</p>
<p class="combat">Leader: <span class="smallcaps">COMBAT SKILL</span> 15   <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> 22</p>
<p class="combat">Soldier 1: <span class="smallcaps">COMBAT SKILL</span> 13   <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> 20</p>
<p class="combat">Soldier 2: <span class="smallcaps">COMBAT SKILL</span> 12   <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> 20</p>
<p class="choice">If you kill all three of them, <a href="sect62.htm">turn to 62</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to evade combat, <a href="sect22.htm">turn to 22</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 181</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />
</head>

<!-- 
   Text copyright © 1984 Joe Dever.
   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.
   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>181</h3>

<p>Instinctively you duck, and dive to avoid the crossbow bolt. The bandit fires and you feel the sleeve of your jacket tear as the missile grazes past your left arm. You thank the gods for your good fortune and sprint on.</p>
<p>None of the other bandits have bows and they soon give up the chase. As you sprint off into the distance, you leave them all far behind.</p>
<p>You stop just long enough to strap up your wounded arm and then continue along the road towards the outer defences of the capital.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect288.htm">Turn to 288</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.<br />

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 182</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />

<!--

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>182</h3>

<p>Three rangers gallop past the river bank, closely followed by the Giaks on their snarling mounts—the Doomwolves. But your Camouflage skill has saved you from being spotted. The pack of evil Giaks continue on their chase without even glancing at the river.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect174.htm">Turn to 174</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 183</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />

<!--

   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.
   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>183</h3>

<p>The officer orders his men to halt and asks you your business. You tell him who you are, and how the monastery has been destroyed. He is deeply saddened to hear your news. He offers you a horse and asks you to accompany him to Prince Pelathar, the King’s son.</p>
<p class="choice">If you accept, <a href="sect97.htm">turn to 97</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you decide to decline his offer, <a href="sect200.htm">turn to 200</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 184</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />
</head>

<!-- 
   Text copyright © 1984 Joe Dever.
   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.
   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>184</h3>

<p>The caravan is out of control and is bumping wildly through the rough ground that borders the highway. With difficulty you eventually steer the frightened horses back onto the road and halt the caravan.</p>
<p>A quick search of the interior reveals 40 Gold Crowns, a Sword, and enough Food for 4 Meals. If you wish to keep any of these items, mark them on your <a href="action.htm">Action Chart</a>.</p>
<p>The fatigue of your ordeal finally catches up with you. You must eat a Meal after which you fall into a deep sleep.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect64.htm">Turn to 64</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 185</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />
</head>

<!-- 
   Text copyright © 1984 Joe Dever.
   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.
   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>185</h3>

<p>You narrow your eyes and scan the trees for some sign of the hidden archer. Your wait is not a long one, for a moment later a sharp pain tears through your chest and you are thrown back by the force of three arrows. Two of the black shafts have sunk deep into your rib cage, and the third has pierced your thigh.</p>
<p>The last thing that you see is the canopy of fern trees above and a large green dragonfly as it settles on your belt buckle.</p>
<p class="deadend">Your life and your mission end here.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>186</h3>

<p>The Kakarmi disappear into the dense undergrowth and you soon find yourself lost. After nearly two hours of walking you hear the sound of running water. You decide to investigate a little closer.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect106.htm">Turn to 106</a>.</p>

</div>

<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>187</h3>

<p>Two furry faces appear over the top of the trunk. Both pairs of eyes stare at your weapon and the two creatures let out a shriek of fright. Leaping from the trunk, they disappear into the forest.</p>
<div class="illustration"><div align="center">
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0">
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpl.png" /></td>

<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="150" width="32" src="brdrl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="[illustration]" border="0" align="middle" height="150" width="386" src="small18.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="150" width="32" src="brdrr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="386" src="brdrbt.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtr.png" /></td>
</tr>
</table>
</div></div>
<p class="choice">If you wish to follow them, <a href="sect186.htm">turn to 186</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to let them go and continue, <a href="sect228.htm">turn to 228</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>188</h3>

<p>You can see the shadow of the Kraan getting larger all around you. It suddenly strikes, pitching you forward onto your face with the power of its attack.</p>
<p>Pick a number from the <a href="random.htm">Random Number Table</a>.</p>
<p>If the number you have picked is 0–6, the Kraan has ripped away your Backpack. You have lost the Pack and all the Equipment that was inside it.</p>
<p>If the number picked is 7–9, your Backpack is intact but you have been wounded in both arms. Lose 3 <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> points and run to the trees.</p>
<p class="choice">Now <a href="sect303.htm">turn to 303</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>189</h3>

<p>You thank your Kai training and your quick thinking, for that bog could have proved as deadly as any Drakkarim or Kraan.</p>
<p>You are worried about losing time, and push on further into the trees towards the south. Ahead of you, you see a wide path that also leads south.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect118.htm">Turn to 118</a>.</p>

</div>

<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>190</h3>

<p>You walk for three miles along the water’s edge until you chance upon a wrecked river barge. It appears to have served as shelter for someone, as you can see a bed and some cooking utensils through a hole in the deck.</p>
<div class="illustration"><div align="center">
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0">
<tr>

<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="150" width="32" src="brdrl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="[illustration]" border="0" align="middle" height="150" width="386" src="small19.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="150" width="32" src="brdrr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="386" src="brdrbt.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtr.png" /></td>
</tr>
</table>
</div></div>
<p class="choice">If you wish to search the barge, <a href="sect20.htm">turn to 20</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to press on, <a href="sect273.htm">turn to 273</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>191</h3>

<p>The bodyguard unsheathes a large scimitar and strikes at your head.</p>
<p class="combat">Bodyguard: <span class="smallcaps">COMBAT SKILL</span> 11   <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> 21</p>
<p class="choice">If you win, <a href="sect24.htm">turn to 24</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to evade more combat during the fight, you can jump from the speeding caravan by <a href="sect234.htm">turning to 234</a>.</p>

</div>

<title>Flight from the Dark: 192</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>192</h3>

<p>You see the razor-fanged mouth of a Doomwolf and hear the hideous cries of the Giaks. Two of them are coming straight for you. You are saved from certain death when your horse jumps at the approaching beasts, knocking them both to the ground. You lash out at the Giak and open a large wound in his head … and then suddenly, as if by a miracle, you’re through and racing on down the highway, clear of the rest of the pack.</p>
<p>But a shadow follows you. It is a Kraan and it has started to dive. Its target is you.</p>
<p class="choice">If you veer off the highway towards the cover of the trees, <a href="sect171.htm">turn to 171</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you press on regardless of the Kraan and gallop flat out down the highway, <a href="sect120.htm">turn to 120</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>193</h3>

<p>The beast and its rider lie dead. You notice a Scroll tucked into the Giak’s belt. You may take this if you wish, but remember to mark it on your <a href="action.htm">Action Chart</a>. The other Doomwolves are charging along the path towards you.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to fight them, <a href="sect253.htm">turn to 253</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to escape into the woods, <a href="sect126.htm">turn to 126</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>194</h3>

<p>You sprint towards the wagon. People are running everywhere in panic as the Kraan make their attack, carrying their poor victims off into the darkening sky. A large Kraan is hovering above the wagon and three snarling Giaks drop from its back onto the startled horses. You must fight them or leave the wagon and run to the safety of a nearby farmhouse.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to fight the Giaks, <a href="sect208.htm">turn to 208</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to run to the farmhouse, <a href="sect148.htm">turn to 148</a>.</p>

</div>

<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>195</h3>

<p>Wiping the bear’s blood from your weapon, you notice the mouth of a cave hidden behind the rock from which the bear attacked.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to investigate this cave further, <a href="sect59.htm">turn to 59</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to press on, <a href="sect106.htm">turn to 106</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>196</h3>

<p>You follow the man into a small library off the main hall. He pushes one of the many books on the shelves which line all four walls, and you hear a metallic <i>click</i>. One section of the bookcase slowly slides back to reveal a hidden passage.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to follow the man into the passage, <a href="sect332.htm">turn to 332</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you do not want to enter the dark corridor, leave the guildhall and return to the street. <a href="sect144.htm">Turn to 144</a>.</p>

</div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 197</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />

<!--

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>197</h3>

<p>The Drakkar lies dead at the bottom of the ferry. He has a Short Sword and 6 Gold Crowns which you may keep if you wish. You push the body into the water where it floats for a few seconds before disappearing into the icy depths.</p>
<p>Grabbing the pole, you steer to the other side of the lake and abandon the ferry.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect172.htm">Turn to 172</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>198</h3>

<p>You can sense that there is someone else behind the screen. There is a lingering aura of wickedness around this shop. Be on your guard—something is wrong here.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to return to the street, <a href="sect7.htm">turn to 7</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to examine the goods in the glass counter, <a href="sect152.htm">turn to 152</a>.</p>

</div>

<title>Flight from the Dark: 199</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>199</h3>

<p>Most of the cupboards and drawers are empty. Whoever lived here took nearly everything they owned with them, but you do manage to scrape together enough fruit in the cellar for one Meal. You may mark this on your <a href="action.htm">Action Chart</a>.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect81.htm">Turn to 81</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>
