<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 200</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>200</h3>

<p>Night is starting to close in. The shadows of the forest are growing longer and darker. Just as you are about to stop and rest, you see through the trees a line of people moving south along a wide highway. Moving closer, you notice a large merchant’s caravan in the centre of the dusty turnpike. It is drawn by six large horses and is moving much faster than any of the other traffic. This could be your chance to reach the capital as quickly as possible.</p>
<div class="illustration"><div align="center">
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0">
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="193" src="brdrtp.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="347" width="32" src="brdrl.png" /></td>
<td><a href="ill12.htm"><img alt="illustration" border="0" align="middle" height="347" width="193" src="ill12.png" /></a></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="347" width="32" src="brdrr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="193" src="brdrbt.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtr.png" /></td>
</tr>
</table>
</div></div>
<p class="choice">If you wish to use the Kai Discipline of Camouflage to hide in among the packing cases strapped to the roof, <a href="sect168.htm">turn to 168</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to jump onto the caravan, <a href="sect78.htm">turn to 78</a>.</p>

</div>

<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>201</h3>

<p>You follow the rough track for nearly an hour when you notice ahead of you another wider path branching off towards the south.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to turn south along the new path, <a href="sect238.htm">turn to 238</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">But if you wish to head east, <a href="sect15.htm">turn to 15</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">Or if you wish to go west, <a href="sect130.htm">turn to 130</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<title>Flight from the Dark: 202</title>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>202</h3>

<p>Urging your horse forward, you gallop down the long stretch of highway towards the capital. After only a few minutes your horse suddenly slows and finally limps to a halt. You dismount and examine its raised right foreleg. You curse your ill luck, for you see that it has thrown a shoe and injured its hoof quite badly. You will have to leave him here and proceed on foot as quickly as you can.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect58.htm">Turn to 58</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.<br />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>203</h3>

<p>You suddenly feel a searing pain shoot through your chest as something explodes against you in a shower of red sparks.</p>
<p>You lose 10 <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> points. Through the smoke, the Sage is preparing to throw more explosives at you.</p>
<p class="choice">If you have 10 or more <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> points left, <a href="sect80.htm">turn to 80</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you now have less than 10 <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> points, <a href="sect344.htm">turn to 344</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.<br />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>204</h3>

<p>After an hour of walking you arrive at a junction. The path continues south and another path joins it from the west. You realize that the west path will lead you back to the marsh, so you continue southwards.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect111.htm">Turn to 111</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 205</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>205</h3>

<p>Their leader picks up your discarded Equipment and ushers you along the road ahead. (You must now erase all Weapons and Backpack Items from your <a href="action.htm">Action Chart</a>.) An evil grin spreads across the face of the other two men, and you suddenly realize that they are not soldiers after all. You make a break for it and run away from there, sprinting towards the distant capital.</p>
<p>Behind you, the ominous <i>click</i> of a crossbow being primed sends a shiver down your spine.</p>
<div class="illustration"><div align="center">
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0">
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpl.png" /></td>

<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="150" width="32" src="brdrl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="[illustration]" border="0" align="middle" height="150" width="386" src="small20.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="150" width="32" src="brdrr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="386" src="brdrbt.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtr.png" /></td>
</tr>
</table>
</div></div>
<p>Pick a number from the <a href="random.htm">Random Number Table</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If the number you have picked is 0–4, <a href="sect181.htm">turn to 181</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If the number is 5–9, <a href="sect145.htm">turn to 145</a>.</p>

</div>

<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>206</h3>

<p>The path soon joins a highway where a signpost indicates Toran to the north and Holmgard to the south. You turn south towards the capital.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect224.htm">Turn to 224</a>.</p>

</div>

<title>Flight from the Dark: 207</title>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>207</h3>

<p>The track soon reaches a larger road which crosses the stream via a stone bridge. A signpost at the bridge points north to Toran and south to Holmgard. The road itself is jammed with people moving south, some pushing their possessions along on handcarts. You join the refugee column and head towards the capital.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect30.htm">Turn to 30</a>.</p>

</div>

   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>208</h3>

<p>The ghoulish creatures thrust their spears at you and attack. Fight these creatures as a single enemy.</p>
<p class="combat">Giaks: <span class="smallcaps">COMBAT SKILL</span> 15   <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> 13</p>
<p class="choice">If you win, you can run to the safety of the farmhouse by <a href="sect148.htm">turning to 148</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">Or you can return to the woods by <a href="sect320.htm">turning to 320</a>.</p>

</div>

<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>209</h3>

<p>You see ahead a corridor sloping upwards, and as you reach the top of this slope, a stone portal slides across to reveal another passage ahead.</p>
<p>You step through the opening which then quickly closes with a crunch.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect23.htm">Turn to 23</a>.</p>

<title>Flight from the Dark: 210</title>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>210</h3>

<p>Just inside the door, you are stopped by a journeyman of the Guildhall and asked to explain your intrusion. You calmly inform him of your urgent message for the King, and he hurries you into the Guildmaster’s chambers.</p>
<p>A distinguished old man in deep purple robes turns to greet you and listens to your story. Taking you by the arm, he leads you into an adjoining library and closes the door. Pressing one of the many thousands of books, he releases a secret panel in the wall and beckons you to follow him.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to follow him into the dark passage, <a href="sect332.htm">turn to 332</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you are not completely happy about this man and wish to leave the Guildhall, <a href="sect37.htm">turn to 37</a>.</p>

</div>

<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>211</h3>

<p>You walk along a dimly lit corridor which opens out into a large square room, with an oak door in the far wall.</p>
<p class="choice">If you possess the Kai Discipline of Sixth Sense <a href="sect244.htm">turn to 244</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to walk across to the door, <a href="sect173.htm">turn to 173</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you would prefer to return to the surface and continue your journey, <a href="sect106.htm">turn to 106</a>.</p>

<title>Flight from the Dark: 212</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>212</h3>

<p>When you awake, the pain is but a memory. Restore all lost <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> points to your original score. A tall man dressed in white robes stands before you, a bowl of herbs in his hands. Placing the leaves into a kettle of boiling water, he then turns to greet you.</p>
<div class="illustration"><div align="center">
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0">
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="193" src="brdrtp.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="337" width="32" src="brdrl.png" /></td>
<td><a href="ill13.htm"><img alt="illustration" border="0" align="middle" height="337" width="193" src="ill13.png" /></a></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="337" width="32" src="brdrr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="193" src="brdrbt.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtr.png" /></td>
</tr>
</table>
</div></div>
<p>‘You have passed close to death and have seen his face, Kai Lord, but the Grey One has not claimed you for his flock. You are healed in body but I sense that you are wounded in spirit. What is it that troubles you so?’</p>
<p>You recognize the man to be one of the King’s senior physicians, for the gold embroidered emblem of a dove upon his sleeve is the sign of his respected vocation. You tell the aged cleric of the events at the monastery and of your perilous journey to the King.</p>
<p>Raising you gently from the bed by your arm, he bids you follow him. You notice that you are in a lavishly decorated room which leads out through a long corridor lined with tapestries. It slowly dawns on you just where you are.</p>
<p>This is the citadel of Holmgard and you are about to meet the King.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect350.htm">Turn to 350</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>213</h3>

<p>You have been trudging through the forest for nearly two hours. The nagging fear that you are lost begins to seem a reality. Apart from the occasional cry of a Kraan in the far distance, you have seen or heard no evidence that the enemy is in this part of the forest. As you descend a rocky hillock, you see something unusual in the tangled woods ahead.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect331.htm">Turn to 331</a>.</p>

</div>

<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>214</h3>

<p>The path gradually narrows until it disappears completely into a mass of dense vegetation. You cannot go any further on this route and therefore you must return to the clearing.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect125.htm">Turn to 125</a> and take the south path.</p>

<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>215</h3>

<p>You emerge into a small clearing. In the centre you see the skeletal remains of a large animal. To the south a narrow track leads off into the distance.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to examine the skeleton, <a href="sect346.htm">turn to 346</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you would rather press on, <a href="sect14.htm">turn to 14</a>.</p>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>216</h3>

<p>Placing one hand on his forehead and the other on his wounded arm, you feel the warmth of your healing powers leave your body and give strength to the injured man.</p>
<p>He tells you his name is Trimis and he is a soldier in Prince Pelathar’s army. The Prince and his troops are engaged in battle to the south, where a large force of the Darklords’ creatures are attacking the bridge of Alema. During the fight, he had been snatched into the air by a Kraan, and dropped into the forest.</p>
<p>You make the soldier as comfortable as possible before continuing on your mission.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect264.htm">Turn to 264</a>.</p>

</div>

<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>217</h3>

<p>You quickly escape from the madman and dodge along a dark alleyway where the houses are small and cramped together. At the very end is a green door with a sign above it that says:</p>
<div class="illustration"><div align="center">
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0">

<td><img alt="[illustration]" border="0" align="middle" height="124" width="386" src="small21.png" /></td>

</tr>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 218</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />
</head>

<!-- 
   Text copyright © 1984 Joe Dever.
   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.
   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>218</h3>

<p>Your senses reveal that more than just horses are heading towards you. You can just make out the very high shrieks of Giak war-cries in the distance. By the number of cries and curses you estimate that there are over a dozen Giaks, and probably Doomwolves as well. You decide that advertising your existence is perhaps not quite such a good idea after all!</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect75.htm">Turn to 75</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>219</h3>

<p>All that remains of you now is embedded five feet into the stairs on which you were standing, beneath a vast granite block.</p>
<p class="deadend">Your mission and your life end here.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>220</h3>

<p>The bodyguard unsheathes a scimitar and lunges for your head.</p>
<p class="combat">Bodyguard: <span class="smallcaps">COMBAT SKILL</span> 11   <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> 20</p>
<p class="choice">If you win, <a href="sect24.htm">turn to 24</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to evade combat at any time during the fight, you can jump from the speeding caravan by <a href="sect234.htm">turning to 234</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>221</h3>

<p>Cautiously, you approach the base of the log wall. The tree trunks are rough-hewn and afford plenty of footholds for your climb. As you reach the top of the wall, you come face to face with a crossbow. The soldier holding it in your face motions for you to descend a wooden ladder to the ground. You do not argue with him. Slowly you descend the ladder.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect318.htm">Turn to 318</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>222</h3>

<p>As you go on you discover a forest path that divides at the point you join it.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to use your Kai Discipline of Tracking, <a href="sect67.htm">turn to 67</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to take the south fork, <a href="sect140.htm">turn to 140</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to take the east fork, <a href="sect252.htm">turn to 252</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>223</h3>

<p>After quite a struggle, you manage to free the heavy trunk from the river bank. Gathering your equipment in a bundle, you stow it on top of the log and then slowly wade out into the river. The current soon takes you and you drift slowly downstream.</p>
<p>After twenty minutes you hear the sound of horses along the left bank.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to hide behind the log, <a href="sect75.htm">turn to 75</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to climb onto the log and prepare to catch the riders’ attention, then <a href="sect175.htm">turn to 175</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>224</h3>

<p>You have ridden several miles and have seen no sign of refugees or of the enemy. You race on towards a high ridge in the middle distance. You should be able to see the capital from there.</p>
<p>As you reach the peak, the sight that meets you on the far side is one of hope—but there is still one challenge you know you have to face.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect153.htm">Turn to 153</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>225</h3>

<p>You recognize the language to be that of the Kakarmi, an intelligent race of forest animals that live in, and care for the forests of Sommerlund. You have nothing to fear from these creatures as they are very timid and gentle in their behaviour. Using your skill of Animal Kinship, you call to them in their strange native tongue.</p>
<p class="choice">If you say ‘Do not be afraid, I am a friend,’ <a href="sect187.htm">turn to 187</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you say ‘I am a Kai Lord. I wish you no harm. I must talk with you,’ <a href="sect39.htm">turn to 39</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>226</h3>

<p>At first the descent is quite easy, but you soon find it difficult to see clearly and your legs feel very weak. The ‘Sleeptooth’ scratches are affecting you, and suddenly you pitch forward and slip head-first into darkness.</p>
<p>Pick a number from the <a href="random.htm">Random Number Table</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If the number you have picked is 0–4, <a href="sect277.htm">turn to 277</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If the number is 5–9, <a href="sect338.htm">turn to 338</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>227</h3>

<p>You are now up to your waist in slimy water. The air is thick with small insects that sting your face and clog your nose. Something wraps itself around your leg. It is a Marshviper and you must fight it.</p>
<p class="combat">Marshviper: <span class="smallcaps">COMBAT SKILL</span> 16   <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> 6</p>
<p class="choice">If you lose any <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> points in the combat, <a href="sect271.htm">turn to 271</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you kill it without losing any <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> points, <a href="sect348.htm">turn to 348</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.<br />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>228</h3>

<p>The path continues eastwards but soon disappears into thick undergrowth.</p>
<p class="choice">If you continue east, cutting through the vegetation with your weapon, <a href="sect140.htm">turn to 140</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you head south to where the bushes are less dense and then press on through the forest, <a href="sect215.htm">turn to 215</a>.</p>

</div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 229</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />

<!--

   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.
   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>229</h3>

<p>The Kraan hovers above you, raising dust with the beat of its huge black wings. The dust gets into your eyes and nose, and you start to cough. Now the beast attacks.</p>
<div class="illustration"><div align="center">
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0">
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="386" src="brdrtp.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="150" width="32" src="brdrl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="[illustration]" border="0" align="middle" height="150" width="386" src="small22.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="150" width="32" src="brdrr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="386" src="brdrbt.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtr.png" /></td>
</tr>
</table>
</div></div>
<p>You must fight it to the death. Because of the dust, you must reduce your <span class="smallcaps">COMBAT SKILL</span> by 1 point.</p>
<p class="combat">Kraan: <span class="smallcaps">COMBAT SKILL</span> 16   <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> 25</p>
<p>If you win you have a choice.</p>
<p class="choice">Will you search the body by <a href="sect267.htm">turning to 267</a>?</p>
<p class="choice">Or will you continue along the east path by <a href="sect125.htm">turning to 125</a>?</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 230</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>230</h3>

<p>In the far distance, you can make out the silhouette of soldiers on barges that are strung out in a line across the river. You can hear the low growls of Doomwolves returning along the opposite bank.</p>
<p>For once you throw caution to the wind and sprint along the river bank towards the barges in the distance.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect179.htm">Turn to 179</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 231</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>231</h3>

<p>You are about to ask the price of the potions when the bamboo screen crashes down and a young man leaps at you. He has a long curved dagger in his hand.</p>
<p>He is upon you and you must fight for your life.</p>
<p class="combat">Robber: <span class="smallcaps">COMBAT SKILL</span> 13   <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> 20</p>
<p class="choice">If you kill him within 4 rounds of combat, <a href="sect94.htm">turn to 94</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you are still fighting after 4 rounds of combat, <a href="sect203.htm">turn to 203</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">You may evade more fighting after 2 rounds of combat by dashing through the front door. If you wish to do this, <a href="sect7.htm">turn to 7</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<title>Flight from the Dark: 232</title>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>232</h3>

<p>The rough-looking leader approaches you and says, ‘Our needs are simple, kind sir. Your money or your life!’</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to fight them, <a href="sect180.htm">turn to 180</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to run, <a href="sect22.htm">turn to 22</a>.</p>

</div>

<title>Flight from the Dark: 233</title>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>233</h3>

<p>After nearly an hour, you catch up with the horse and succeed in calming him down. You are now north of the cabin, but you are confident of finding your way back.</p>
<p>Mounting the horse, you ride back past the cabin, and press on towards the south once again.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect206.htm">Turn to 206</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 234</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>234</h3>

<p>You jump clear of the speeding caravan but land very badly and break your ankle. The pain is terrible and you soon lose consciousness.</p>
<p>Unfortunately you never wake up, but it may be of interest to you that your head is now adorning the saddle of a Kraan.</p>
<p class="deadend">Your life and your mission end here.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.<br />

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 235</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>235</h3>

<p>The Prince’s horse is indeed a magnificent animal, fast and sure of foot. You gallop along the twisting track as if it were a straight highway, until the noise of battle has disappeared far behind you.</p>
<p>You are hungry and must eat a Meal during your ride.</p>
<p>After several miles, the path stops abruptly at a junction. There is a signpost, but it has been hacked down.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to use your Kai Discipline of Tracking, <a href="sect254.htm">turn to 254</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to turn left, <a href="sect32.htm">go to 32</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to turn right, <a href="sect146.htm">go to 146</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>
</div><p class="copyright">
   Text copyright © 1984 Joe Dever.<br />
   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.<br />
  </p>

</div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 236</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />

<!--

   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>236</h3>

<p>The Gem hovers above the mouth of the skeleton king, glowing a fierce red. Suddenly, an explosion of searing crimson flame lashes upwards from the sarcophagus, destroying the Gem completely. You are thrown against the far wall and knocked unconscious.</p>
<div class="illustration"><div align="center">
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0">
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="386" src="brdrtp.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="150" width="32" src="brdrl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="[illustration]" border="0" align="middle" height="150" width="386" src="small23.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="150" width="32" src="brdrr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="386" src="brdrbt.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtr.png" /></td>
</tr>
</table>
</div></div>
<p>When you awake, the chamber is completely empty. The skeleton king and the sarcophagus have vanished. You have lost 6 <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> points, and your initial <span class="smallcaps">COMBAT SKILL</span> is reduced by 1 point for the rest of your life. (Remember to erase the Vordak Gem from your <a href="action.htm">Action Chart</a>. If you had two Gems, you need erase only one.)</p>
<p>You carefully get to your feet and stagger towards the tunnel.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect104.htm">Turn to 104</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.<br />

<title>Flight from the Dark: 237</title>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>237</h3>

<p>You make full use of your Kai Discipline and quickly burrow deep into the loose earth of the wooded hillside. Covering yourself with your cloak, you pull a loose branch across your hastily dug shelter.</p>
<p>Pick a number from the <a href="random.htm">Random Number Table</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you have picked a number 0–4, then you have passed undetected. <a href="sect265.htm">Turn to 265</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you have picked a number 5–9, then you are not so lucky! <a href="sect72.htm">Turn to 72</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 238</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />

<!--

   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.
   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>238</h3>

<p>The path meanders between several small, wooded hills and eventually leads to a ruined log cabin. It seems that it had burnt down not so long ago, for the ashes are still warm and a haze of smoke still lingers. You sense possible danger here.</p>
<div class="illustration"><div align="center">
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0">
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="386" src="brdrtp.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="150" width="32" src="brdrl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="[illustration]" border="0" align="middle" height="150" width="386" src="small24.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="150" width="32" src="brdrr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="386" src="brdrbt.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtr.png" /></td>
</tr>
</table>
</div></div>
<p class="choice">You may leave by the south route by <a href="sect42.htm">turning to 42</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">Or you may take the north track by <a href="sect68.htm">turning to 68</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 239</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />

<!--

   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.
   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>239</h3>

<p>As you push on into the forest, you hear the wings of the Kraan pass above the trees and disappear northwards. You ride on for nearly an hour until you come to a clearing. On the far side is a track that leads off to the south.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to enter the clearing and take the south exit, <a href="sect34.htm">turn to 34</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you would rather skirt the edge of the clearing and pick up the track further on, <a href="sect118.htm">turn to 118</a>.</p>

</div>

<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>240</h3>

<p>The path leads along a ridge of wooded hillocks and changes direction towards the east.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect79.htm">Turn to 79</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<title>Flight from the Dark: 241</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>241</h3>

<p>The wizard heeds your cry and spins around just in time to loose a searing bolt of energy at the Giak. The creature’s head disintegrates in flames and its twitching body falls in a heap at the foot of the pillar. The Giak officer sees you and shouts, <i xml:lang="x-giak">‘Ogot … Ogot!’</i> to his cowering troops, who quickly run away from the ruins to the safety of the forest beyond.</p>
<p>The young wizard wipes his brow, and walks towards you, his hand extended in gratitude and friendship.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect349.htm">Turn to 349</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>242</h3>

<p>The lid of the sarcophagus slips to the floor with a dull crunch. You are looking at the remains of an ancient king, who lies still surrounded by his treasure. An ornate crown is still in position on his skull. The jaw of the skeleton is wide open and the darkness of the mouth seems strangely bottomless. A distant rumbling can now be heard from deep in the earth.</p>
<p class="choice">If you have the Kai Discipline of Mindshield, <a href="sect166.htm">turn to 166</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you do not, <a href="sect9.htm">turn to 9</a>.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 243</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />

<!--

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>243</h3>

<p>Hurrying through the forest, you stumble and fall down a steep slope which drops you in a heap on a hidden path below. On the path is a dead body. It is a Giak, a spiteful and ghoulish servant of the Darklords. Many centuries ago, their ancestors were used by the Darklords to build for them the infernal city of Helgedad, which lies in the volcanic wastelands beyond the Durncrag range of mountains. The construction of the city was a long and torturous nightmare, and only the strongest of the Giaks survived the heat and poisonous atmospheres of Helgedad. This creature that lies before you is a descendant of these Giak slaves. It has been killed by a sword blow to its head, and by its side lies a Mace. You may take this Weapon if you wish.</p>
<p class="choice">Continue along the hidden path by <a href="sect97.htm">turning to 97</a>.</p>

</div>

<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>244</h3>

<p>Your senses tell you that you are not alone. You are in very great danger. Return to the surface as quickly as you can.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect93.htm">Turn to 93</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>245</h3>

<p>Arrows hit the water above you, and drop harmlessly past as you swim beneath the surface towards the opposite bank.</p>
<p>Quickly you wade out of the river and dash for the trees. You are now out of range of the Giaks, who remount their Doomwolves and continue their chase.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect190.htm">Turn to 190</a>.</p>

</div>

<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>246</h3>

<p>When the ferry reaches the middle of the lake, the man stops rowing and stands up. He laughs menacingly and pulls back the hood of his cloak to reveal himself. He is a Drakkar and you must fight him.</p>
<div class="illustration"><div align="center">

<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>247</h3>

<p>The merchant looks angry. He calls to his bodyguard. You must think of something quickly.</p>
<p class="choice">If you decide to offer him something of greater value that you have in your Backpack, <a href="sect159.htm">turn to 159</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you prepare to fight the bodyguard, <a href="sect220.htm">turn to 220</a>.</p>

</div>

<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>248</h3>

<p>You reach the base of the hill and hurry into the forest. After only a few minutes you discover an old forest track.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to follow this track north, <a href="sect44.htm">turn to 44</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to follow this track east, <a href="sect300.htm">turn to 300</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>249</h3>

<p>You descend a flight of stone stairs that lead to a large chamber. A macabre sight awaits you. Directly opposite, across the large stone room, is an ornate archway with a corridor leading into the darkness beyond. The strange green light radiates from two lines of skulls each resting on a stone plinth. They face each other to form an eerie walkway across the room.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to walk across the room to the archway, <a href="sect169.htm">turn to 169</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to attack the skulls, <a href="sect107.htm">turn to 107</a>.</p>

</div>

<title>Flight from the Dark: 250</title>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>250</h3>

<p>Leaping from the top of the trunk, you land in front of two small furry creatures. You recognize that they are Kakarmi, an intelligent race of animals that inhabit and tend the forests of Sommerlund. Before you can apologize for your dramatic entrance, the frightened little creatures scurry off into the forest.</p>
<div class="illustration"><div align="center">
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0">
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpl.png" /></td>

<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="150" width="32" src="brdrl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="[illustration]" border="0" align="middle" height="150" width="386" src="small25.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="150" width="32" src="brdrr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="386" src="brdrbt.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtr.png" /></td>
</tr>
</table>
</div></div>
<p class="choice">If you wish to follow them, <a href="sect186.htm">turn to 186</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to continue, <a href="sect228.htm">turn to 228</a>.</p>

</div>

<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>251</h3>

<p>You are lucky, they do not seem to have spotted you. They slowly move on and have soon disappeared along the far side of the ridge. You continue your run.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect10.htm">Turn to 10</a>.</p>

</div>

<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>252</h3>

<p>In the centre of a small clearing you see a group of humans talking excitedly and gesturing wildly with their hands. There are two children, three men, and a woman. Their belongings are wrapped in bundles which they carry slung over their shoulders. Their clothes look well made and expensive but they are dirty and torn.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to approach them and ask who they are, <a href="sect155.htm">turn to 155</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to avoid them and continue onwards on your mission, <a href="sect70.htm">turn to 70</a>.</p>

</div>

<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>253</h3>

<p>The Doomwolves are soon on you and you must fight them one at a time.</p>
<p class="combat">Doomwolf 1: <span class="smallcaps">COMBAT SKILL</span> 13   <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> 24</p>
<p class="combat">Doomwolf 2: <span class="smallcaps">COMBAT SKILL</span> 14   <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> 23</p>
<p class="combat">Doomwolf 3: <span class="smallcaps">COMBAT SKILL</span> 14   <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> 22</p>
<p class="combat">Doomwolf 4: <span class="smallcaps">COMBAT SKILL</span> 15   <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> 21</p>
<p class="choice">If you kill them all in battle, <a href="sect278.htm">turn to 278</a>.</p>

</div>

<title>Flight from the Dark: 254</title>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>254</h3>

<p>Your Tracking ability tells you that several trails from the right path lead off in the direction of the left path. They have been made by large wolves. The Darklords use such beasts to scout for their armies. They are vicious creatures and are often ridden by Giaks. The left path leads towards Holmgard, and the right path leads off towards the Durncrag Mountains. The choice of route is yours.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to turn left, <a href="sect32.htm">go to 32</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to turn right, <a href="sect146.htm">go to 146</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>255</h3>

<p>The creature that you now face is a Gourgaz, one of a race of cold-blooded reptilian creatures that dwell deep in the treacherous Maakenmire swamps. Their favourite food is human flesh!</p>
<p>The Prince’s Sword lies at your feet. You may pick up and use this weapon if you wish. The Gourgaz is about to strike at you—you must fight him to the death.</p>
<p class="combat">Gourgaz: <span class="smallcaps">COMBAT SKILL</span> 20   <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> 30</p>
<p>This creature is immune to Mindblast.</p>
<p class="choice">If you win, <a href="sect82.htm">turn to 82</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>256</h3>

<p>You are awoken by the cries of Kraan high above you in the clear morning sky. Rubbing your eyes, you peer upwards through the canopy of branches to see three of the loathsome creatures fly off towards the north.</p>
<p>You are sure you have not been spotted, but perhaps it would be best to leave now—just in case. You mount your horse and ride south along the highway.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect224.htm">Turn to 224</a>.</p>

</div>

<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>257</h3>

<p>You find a stone portal in the east wall, but there does not appear to be any way of opening it.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to examine the statue, <a href="sect133.htm">turn to 133</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to sit on the seat, <a href="sect161.htm">turn to 161</a>.</p>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 258</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>258</h3>

<p>Using your Kai Discipline of Mind Over Matter, you untie the ropes binding your hands. You wait for a chance to make a break for it and then sprint as fast as you can into the dense undergrowth. Black arrows whistle past you, but you are soon deep among the trees and safe again. You have lost your Backpack and Weapons but you have your life and limbs intact. You continue to push on into the forest.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect50.htm">Turn to 50</a>.</p>

</div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 259</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />

<!-- 
   Text copyright © 1984 Joe Dever.
   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.
   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>259</h3>

<p>The room is getting colder. You gradually notice the smell of sulphur in the air. You can hear chanting in the distance. It sounds as if it is somewhere in another part of this cave. A slit in the stone wall opens, and the end of a black staff begins to appear. Suddenly a bolt of blue lightning leaps from the staff and hits you in the chest.</p>
<p>As your life slowly drains away, the last thing you see is an old man dressed in black robes raising a dagger above your throat.</p>
<p class="deadend">Your life and your mission end here.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 260</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />
</head>

<!--

   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.
   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>260</h3>

<p>Swimming towards the bank, you can see the ranger spread-eagled at the water’s edge. You reach him but only to find that he has broken his neck in the fall and is dead.</p>
<p>Suddenly, two Giaks jump on you from above and you must fight them. You are unarmed and must fight the Giaks with your bare hands. Deduct 4 points from your <span class="smallcaps">COMBAT SKILL</span> and fight them one at a time.</p>
<p class="combat">Giak 1: <span class="smallcaps">COMBAT SKILL</span> 11   <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> 18</p>
<p class="combat">Giak 2: <span class="smallcaps">COMBAT SKILL</span> 12   <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> 17</p>
<p class="choice">If you win, <a href="sect156.htm">turn to 156</a>.</p>

</div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 261</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>261</h3>

<p>Sweating, and out of breath, you part the dense undergrowth to see a Kraan hovering over the wagon. Three ghoulish Giaks drop from its back, startling the horses. They advance upon the helpless children with their spears.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to run back to the wagon and defend the children, <a href="sect208.htm">turn to 208</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you want to run deeper into the forest, <a href="sect264.htm">turn to 264</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>262</h3>

<p>The merchant takes your Gold and clicks his fingers. His bodyguard attacks you with his scimitar.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to fight, <a href="sect191.htm">turn to 191</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to evade combat, jump clear of the speeding caravan by <a href="sect234.htm">turning to 234</a>.</p>

</div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 263</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />

   Text copyright © 1984 Joe Dever.
   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.
   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>263</h3>

<p>Carefully, you follow the stream as it makes its way towards the east. Suddenly you notice something in the distance that brings you to a halt.</p>
<p>Lying in the rushing water like a great black dam is a dead Kraan. You creep nearer, under cover of the foliage, until you see three arrows deep in the beast’s chest. Trapped beneath the beast is the body of its rider. It is a Giak, a spiteful and malicious servant of the Darklords. Many centuries ago, their ancestors were used by the Darklords to build the infernal city of Helgedad, which lies in the volcanic wastelands beyond the Durncrag range of mountains. The construction of the city was a long and torturous nightmare, and only the strongest Giaks survived the heat and poisonous atmospheres of Helgedad. This creature is a descendant of these Giak slaves. It seems that this one must have drowned. The Giak’s pouch contains 3 Gold Crowns. (You may take these if you wish.)</p>
<div class="illustration"><div align="center">
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0">
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="386" src="brdrtp.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="150" width="32" src="brdrl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="[illustration]" border="0" align="middle" height="150" width="386" src="small26.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="150" width="32" src="brdrr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="386" src="brdrbt.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtr.png" /></td>
</tr>
</table>
</div></div>
<p class="choice">You may continue downstream, by <a href="sect70.htm">turning to 70</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">Or you may leave the stream and make your way on foot through the wooded hills to the south by <a href="sect157.htm">turning to 157</a>.</p>

</div>

<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>264</h3>

<p>You have not gone far when you hear the sound of battle to the west.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to follow the sound, <a href="sect97.htm">turn to 97</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you would rather continue south, <a href="sect6.htm">turn to 6</a>.</p>

<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>265</h3>

<p>You quickly move off into the forest before more Doomwolves or Kraan appear.</p>
<p>You have walked for more than an hour when you reach the top of a rocky hill. The sight that befalls you on the other side is one of hope. But there is also a daunting challenge to be faced.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect142.htm">Turn to 142</a>.</p>

</div>

<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>266</h3>

<p>As the beast writhes in its final death agony on the black stone floor, the portal in the east wall clicks open to reveal a corridor beyond. You quickly dash through the secret door just as it crashes shut.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect209.htm">Turn to 209</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>267</h3>

<p>Covering your nose with your cloak, you cautiously approach the dead beast. The sharp smell of its fetid black blood makes your stomach churn, but you are determined to press on. Then you notice a large saddlebag strapped to its chest. Opening the bag, you find a Message written on an animal skin.</p>
<div class="illustration"><div align="center">
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0">
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpl.png" /></td>

<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrtpr.png" /></td>

<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="324" width="32" src="brdrl.png" /></td>
<td><a href="ill15.htm"><img alt="illustration" border="0" align="middle" height="324" width="193" src="ill15.png" /></a></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="324" width="32" src="brdrr.png" /></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtl.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="193" src="brdrbt.png" /></td>
<td><img alt="" align="middle" height="32" width="32" src="brdrbtr.png" /></td>
</tr>
</table>
</div></div>
<p>Deeper in the bag is a Dagger. You may keep both the Message and the Dagger if you wish.</p>
<p>You leave the body and continue eastwards along the path.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect125.htm">Turn to 125</a>.</p>

</div>

<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>268</h3>

<p>You black out for only a few minutes before you are revived with a measure of strong spirit. Feeling weary but thankful to be alive, you lean on the shoulders of the King’s men and you stagger towards the outer defences.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect288.htm">Turn to 288</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>269</h3>

<p>The madman lies dead at your feet. Two soldiers soon appear at the doorway and immediately congratulate you. They tell you that he was an escaped lunatic whom they had been tracking for the last two days. One of the soldiers gives you 10 Gold Crowns reward money and offers to escort you to the citadel.</p>
<p class="choice">If you accept his offer, <a href="sect314.htm">turn to 314</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you would prefer to trust your own sense of direction, <a href="sect7.htm">turn to 7</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>270</h3>

<p>You hear the angry cries of the enemy drift across the lake. You must leave here before more Kraan appear. You mount your steed and push on further into the forest.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect21.htm">Turn to 21</a>.</p>

</div>

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 271</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />

<!--

   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>271</h3>

<p>You feel very weak. The poison of the snake has entered your bloodstream and you can feel the muscles of your body involuntarily tightening and relaxing. Your legs suddenly collapse beneath you and you feel the slimy water of the marsh close over your head.</p>
<p class="deadend">Your life ends here.</p>

</div>
<div class="navigation"><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="left.png" /><a href="toc.htm"><img alt="Table of Contents" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="toc.png" /></a><img alt="" border="0" height="30" width="150" src="right.png" /></div>

</html><!DOCTYPE html PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD XHTML 1.0 Transitional//EN" "http://www.w3.org/TR/xhtml1/DTD/xhtml1-transitional.dtd">

<head>
<title>Flight from the Dark: 272</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />
<meta content="noindex,nofollow" name="robots" />
<link type="text/css" href="main.css" rel="stylesheet" />
</head>

<!-- 
   Text copyright © 1984 Joe Dever.
   Illustrations copyright © 1984 Gary Chalk.
   Published by Project Aon. -->

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>272</h3>

<p>Keeping a watchful eye on the sky above, you move quickly along the track. You recall that this route leads to Fogwood, a small cluster of huts that have been used by a family of charcoal burners for nearly fifty years. After twenty minutes you reach the edge of a clearing where the huts are grouped in a small circle. There is no sign of the usual mist of wood smoke which gives Fogwood its apt name, and the huts are unusually quiet.</p>
<p class="choice">If you have the Kai Discipline of Tracking, you may <a href="sect134.htm">turn to 134</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you do not possess this skill, you prepare your weapon and stealthily approach the huts. <a href="sect305.htm">Turn to 305</a>.</p>

</div>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>273</h3>

<p>The outer fieldworks of the city can now be seen. Drawn across the river is a line of barges chained together to form a floating barricade. You can also see soldiers running along the log walls of the fieldworks, and you can hear the faint noise of battle drifting from the west.</p>
<div class="illustration"><div align="center">
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0">

</tr>

<p class="choice">If you wish to approach the barges, <a href="sect179.htm">turn to 179</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If you wish to take cover in the trees, <a href="sect51.htm">turn to 51</a>.</p>

<title>Flight from the Dark: 274</title>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>274</h3>

<p>In your haste to avoid the enemy, you catch your foot in a tree root and you are pitched head over heels in a tumble of dust and leaves. You quickly get to your feet and, crashing through the undergrowth at the base of the hill, you run into the forest. You have been running for nearly ten minutes when you discover that you have lost your Weapon(s). Well, at least you still have your life and your Backpack. Wiping the grime from your face, you push on through the trees ahead.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect331.htm">Turn to 331</a>.</p>

</div>

<title>Flight from the Dark: 275</title>
<meta content="text/html; charset=utf-8" http-equiv="Content-type" />

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>275</h3>

<p>You have followed this twisting track for about twenty minutes when you hear the beating of wings high above the trees. Looking up you see a large Kraan approaching from the north, its huge black wings casting a gigantic shadow on the trees below.</p>
<p>On its back are two creatures armed with long spears. They are Mountain Giaks—small ugly creatures full of hatred and malice. Many centuries ago, their ancestors were used by the Darklords to build the infernal city of Helgedad, which lies in the volcanic wastelands beyond the Durncrag mountain range. The construction of the city was long and torturous, and only the strongest of the creatures survived the heat and poisonous atmosphere of Helgedad.</p>
<p>Quickly you dive for the shelter of a large fern tree as the Kraan passes overhead. With heart pounding, you pray that your quick reactions have saved you from being spotted.</p>
<p>Pick a number from the <a href="random.htm">Random Number Table</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If the number you have picked is 0–4, <a href="sect345.htm">turn to 345</a>.</p>
<p class="choice">If the number is 5–9, <a href="sect74.htm">turn to 74</a>.</p>

</div>

<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>276</h3>

<p>Reaching for your weapon you manage to hack your way through the tangle of wood and twisted branches to the clearer forest beyond. Your cloak is torn in several places and your right leg is badly bruised above the knee.</p>
<p class="choice">Lose 1 <span class="smallcaps">ENDURANCE</span> point and <a href="sect213.htm">turn to 213</a>.</p>

<body text="#003300" bgcolor="#ffffe6" background="bckgrnd.png" link="#006633" alink="#006633" vlink="#006633">
<div id="title"><img usemap="#imagemap" align="middle" border="0" height="100" width="550" src="title.png" alt="Flight from the Dark" /></div>
<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>277</h3>

<p>When you awake, you find yourself lying at the foot of a steep slope in a tangle of tall grasses. Your Backpack and Weapon are missing and your head aches. You cannot tell how long you have been unconscious, but you realize that you must not delay in pressing on with your mission.</p>
<p>Standing up, you see your Backpack is intact but the Weapon is broken in two and is now useless. Remember to cross it off your <a href="action.htm">Action Chart</a>. (If you have more than one weapon, only one of them is broken—you may choose which one it is.) You quickly pick up your Backpack and move off into the trees ahead.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect113.htm">Turn to 113</a>.</p>

</div>

<div id="body">
<div class="numbered">
<div class="maintext">
<h3>278</h3>

<p>You quickly leave the path and gallop off along the track heading towards the capital. When you reach the point where the Doomwolves stopped, you can see just beyond a meadow the main highway which runs from the northern port of Toran to Holmgard. You should reach the capital by morning.</p>
<p class="choice"><a href="sect149.htm">Turn to 149</a>.</p>

</div>
